3475             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3476         }
3477         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3478         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3479           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3480           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3481           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible annotation");
3482         }
3483         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3484 
3485       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3486         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3487           classfile_parse_error(
3488             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3489         }
3490         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3491         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3492 
3493         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible type annotation");
3494         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3495         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length);
3496 
3497       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3498         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3499           classfile_parse_error(
3500             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3501         }
3502         runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3503         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3504           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3505           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3506           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible type annotation");
3507         }
3508         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3509 
3510       } else {
3511         // Skip unknown attributes
3512         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3513       }
3514       calculate_attr_size += attribute_length;
3515     } // End of attributes For loop
3516 
3517     AnnotationArray* annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3518                                                         runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3519                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations,
3520                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3521                                                         CHECK_0);
3522     AnnotationArray* type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3523                                                              runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3524                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3525                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3526                                                              CHECK_0);
3527 
3528     RecordComponent* record_component =
3529       RecordComponent::allocate(_loader_data, name_index, descriptor_index,
3530                                 attributes_count, generic_sig_index,
3531                                 annotations, type_annotations, CHECK_0);
3532     record_components->at_put(x, record_component);
3533   }  // End of component processing loop
3534 
3535   // Restore buffer's current position.
3536   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3537   return calculate_attr_size;
3538 }
3539 
3540 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(TRAPS) {
3541   set_class_synthetic_flag(true);
3542 }
3543 
3544 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_signature_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs, TRAPS) {
3545   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3546 
3547   const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2(CHECK);
3548   check_property(
3549     valid_symbol_at(signature_index),
3550     "Invalid constant pool index %u in Signature attribute in class file %s",
3551     signature_index, CHECK);
3552   set_class_generic_signature_index(signature_index);
3553 }
3554 
3555 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3556                                                                   ConstantPool* cp,
3557                                                                   u4 attribute_byte_length,
3558                                                                   TRAPS) {
3559   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3560   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3561 
3562   const u1* const current_start = cfs->current();
3563 
3564   guarantee_property(attribute_byte_length >= sizeof(u2),
3565                      "Invalid BootstrapMethods attribute length %u in class file %s",
3566                      attribute_byte_length,
3567                      CHECK);
3568 
3569   cfs->guarantee_more(attribute_byte_length, CHECK);
3570 
3571   const int attribute_array_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3572 
3573   guarantee_property(_max_bootstrap_specifier_index < attribute_array_length,
3574                      "Short length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3575                      CHECK);
3576 
3577 
3578   // The attribute contains a counted array of counted tuples of shorts,
3579   // represending bootstrap specifiers:
3580   //    length*{bootstrap_method_index, argument_count*{argument_index}}
3581   const int operand_count = (attribute_byte_length - sizeof(u2)) / sizeof(u2);
3582   // operand_count = number of shorts in attr, except for leading length
3583 
3584   // The attribute is copied into a short[] array.
3585   // The array begins with a series of short[2] pairs, one for each tuple.
3586   const int index_size = (attribute_array_length * 2);
3587 
3588   Array<u2>* const operands =
3589     MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, index_size + operand_count, CHECK);
3590 
3591   // Eagerly assign operands so they will be deallocated with the constant
3592   // pool if there is an error.
3593   cp->set_operands(operands);
3594 
3595   int operand_fill_index = index_size;
3596   const int cp_size = cp->length();
3597 
3598   for (int n = 0; n < attribute_array_length; n++) {
3599     // Store a 32-bit offset into the header of the operand array.
3600     ConstantPool::operand_offset_at_put(operands, n, operand_fill_index);
3601 
3602     // Read a bootstrap specifier.
3603     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * 2, CHECK);  // bsm, argc
3604     const u2 bootstrap_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3605     const u2 argument_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3606     check_property(
3607       valid_cp_range(bootstrap_method_index, cp_size) &&
3608       cp->tag_at(bootstrap_method_index).is_method_handle(),
3609       "bootstrap_method_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3610       bootstrap_method_index,
3611       CHECK);
3612 
3613     guarantee_property((operand_fill_index + 1 + argument_count) < operands->length(),
3614       "Invalid BootstrapMethods num_bootstrap_methods or num_bootstrap_arguments value in class file %s",
3615       CHECK);
3616 
3617     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, bootstrap_method_index);
3618     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_count);
3619 
3620     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * argument_count, CHECK);  // argv[argc]
3621     for (int j = 0; j < argument_count; j++) {
3622       const u2 argument_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3623       check_property(
3624         valid_cp_range(argument_index, cp_size) &&
3625         cp->tag_at(argument_index).is_loadable_constant(),
3626         "argument_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3627         argument_index,
3628         CHECK);
3629       operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_index);
3630     }
3631   }
3632   guarantee_property(current_start + attribute_byte_length == cfs->current(),
3633                      "Bad length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3634                      CHECK);
3635 }
3636 
3637 bool ClassFileParser::supports_records() {
3638   return _major_version == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
3639     _minor_version == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
3640     Arguments::enable_preview();
3641 }
3642 
3643 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_attributes(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3644                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
3645                  ClassFileParser::ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
3646                                                  TRAPS) {
3647   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3648   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3649   assert(parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
3650 
3651   // Set inner classes attribute to default sentinel
3652   _inner_classes = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3653   // Set nest members attribute to default sentinel
3654   _nest_members = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3655   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // attributes_count
3656   u2 attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3657   bool parsed_sourcefile_attribute = false;
3658   bool parsed_innerclasses_attribute = false;
3659   bool parsed_nest_members_attribute = false;
3660   bool parsed_nest_host_attribute = false;
3661   bool parsed_record_attribute = false;
3662   bool parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = false;
3663   bool parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = false;
3664   const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
3665   int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
3666   const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
3667   int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
3668   const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
3669   int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3670   const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
3671   int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3672   bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
3673   bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
3674   bool parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = false;
3675   const u1* inner_classes_attribute_start = NULL;
3676   u4  inner_classes_attribute_length = 0;
3677   u2  enclosing_method_class_index = 0;
3678   u2  enclosing_method_method_index = 0;
3679   const u1* nest_members_attribute_start = NULL;
3680   u4  nest_members_attribute_length = 0;
3681   const u1* record_attribute_start = NULL;
3682   u4  record_attribute_length = 0;
3683 
3684   // Iterate over attributes
3685   while (attributes_count--) {
3686     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK);  // attribute_name_index, attribute_length
3687     const u2 attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3688     const u4 attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
3689     check_property(
3690       valid_symbol_at(attribute_name_index),
3691       "Attribute name has bad constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3692       attribute_name_index, CHECK);
3693     const Symbol* const tag = cp->symbol_at(attribute_name_index);
3694     if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_file()) {
3695       // Check for SourceFile tag
3696       if (_need_verify) {
3697         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong SourceFile attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3698       }
3699       if (parsed_sourcefile_attribute) {
3700         classfile_parse_error("Multiple SourceFile attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3701       } else {
3702         parsed_sourcefile_attribute = true;
3703       }
3704       parse_classfile_sourcefile_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3705     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_debug_extension()) {
3706       // Check for SourceDebugExtension tag
3707       if (parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist) {
3708           classfile_parse_error(
3709             "Multiple SourceDebugExtension attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3710       }
3711       parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = true;
3712       parse_classfile_source_debug_extension_attribute(cfs, (int)attribute_length, CHECK);
3713     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_inner_classes()) {
3714       // Check for InnerClasses tag
3715       if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute) {
3716         classfile_parse_error("Multiple InnerClasses attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3717       } else {
3718         parsed_innerclasses_attribute = true;
3719       }
3720       inner_classes_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3721       inner_classes_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3722       cfs->skip_u1(inner_classes_attribute_length, CHECK);
3723     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_synthetic()) {
3724       // Check for Synthetic tag
3725       // Shouldn't we check that the synthetic flags wasn't already set? - not required in spec
3726       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3727         classfile_parse_error(
3728           "Invalid Synthetic classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3729           attribute_length, CHECK);
3730       }
3731       parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(CHECK);
3732     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_deprecated()) {
3733       // Check for Deprecatd tag - 4276120
3734       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3735         classfile_parse_error(
3736           "Invalid Deprecated classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3737           attribute_length, CHECK);
3738       }
3739     } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3740       if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
3741         if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
3742           classfile_parse_error(
3743             "Multiple Signature attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3744         }
3745         if (attribute_length != 2) {
3746           classfile_parse_error(
3747             "Wrong Signature attribute length %u in class file %s",
3748             attribute_length, CHECK);
3749         }
3750         parse_classfile_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3751       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
3752         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
3753           classfile_parse_error(
3754             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3755         }
3756         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3757         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
3758         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null visible annotations");
3759         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK);
3760         parse_annotations(cp,
3761                           runtime_visible_annotations,
3762                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3763                           parsed_annotations,
3764                           _loader_data,
3765                           CHECK);
3766         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3767       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3768         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3769           classfile_parse_error(
3770             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3771         }
3772         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3773         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3774           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3775           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3776           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null invisible annotations");
3777         }
3778         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3779       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_enclosing_method()) {
3780         if (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3781           classfile_parse_error("Multiple EnclosingMethod attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3782         } else {
3783           parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = true;
3784         }
3785         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 4,
3786           "Wrong EnclosingMethod attribute length %u in class file %s",
3787           attribute_length, CHECK);
3788         cfs->guarantee_more(4, CHECK);  // class_index, method_index
3789         enclosing_method_class_index  = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3790         enclosing_method_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3791         if (enclosing_method_class_index == 0) {
3792           classfile_parse_error("Invalid class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3793         }
3794         // Validate the constant pool indices and types
3795         check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(enclosing_method_class_index),
3796           "Invalid or out-of-bounds class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3797         if (enclosing_method_method_index != 0 &&
3798             (!cp->is_within_bounds(enclosing_method_method_index) ||
3799              !cp->tag_at(enclosing_method_method_index).is_name_and_type())) {
3800           classfile_parse_error("Invalid or out-of-bounds method index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3801         }
3802       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_bootstrap_methods() &&
3803                  _major_version >= Verifier::INVOKEDYNAMIC_MAJOR_VERSION) {
3804         if (parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute) {
3805           classfile_parse_error("Multiple BootstrapMethods attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3806         }
3807         parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = true;
3808         parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(cfs, cp, attribute_length, CHECK);
3809       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3810         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3811           classfile_parse_error(
3812             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3813         }
3814         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3815         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3816         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null visible type annotations");
3817         // No need for the VM to parse Type annotations
3818         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK);
3819       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3820         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3821           classfile_parse_error(
3822             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3823         } else {
3824           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3825         }
3826         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3827           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3828           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3829           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null invisible type annotations");
3830         }
3831         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3832       } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION) {
3833         if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_members()) {
3834           // Check for NestMembers tag
3835           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3836             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3837           } else {
3838             parsed_nest_members_attribute = true;
3839           }
3840           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3841             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestHost and NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3842           }
3843           nest_members_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3844           nest_members_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3845           cfs->skip_u1(nest_members_attribute_length, CHECK);
3846         } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_host()) {
3847           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3848             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3849           } else {
3850             parsed_nest_host_attribute = true;
3851           }
3852           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3853             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestMembers and NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3854           }
3855           if (_need_verify) {
3856             guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong NestHost attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3857           }
3858           cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);
3859           u2 class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3860           check_property(
3861                          valid_klass_reference_at(class_info_index),
3862                          "Nest-host class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3863                          class_info_index, CHECK);
3864           _nest_host = class_info_index;
3865         } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION) {
3866           if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_record()) {
3867             // Skip over Record attribute if not supported or if super class is
3868             // not java.lang.Record.
3869             if (supports_records() &&
3870                 cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index) == vmSymbols::java_lang_Record()) {
3871               if (parsed_record_attribute) {
3872                 classfile_parse_error("Multiple Record attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3873               }
3874               // Check that class is final and not abstract.
3875               if (!_access_flags.is_final() || _access_flags.is_abstract()) {
3876                 classfile_parse_error("Record attribute in non-final or abstract class file %s", CHECK);
3877               }
3878               parsed_record_attribute = true;
3879               record_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3880               record_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3881             } else if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, record)) {
3882               // Log why the Record attribute was ignored.  Note that if the
3883               // class file version is JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION.65535 and
3884               // --enable-preview wasn't specified then a java.lang.UnsupportedClassVersionError
3885               // exception would have been thrown.
3886               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
3887               if (supports_records()) {
3888                 log_info(class, record)(
3889                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because super type is not java.lang.Record",
3890                   _class_name->as_C_string());
3891               } else {
3892                 log_info(class, record)(
3893                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because class file version is not %d.65535",
3894                    _class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
3895               }
3896             }
3897             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3898           } else {
3899             // Unknown attribute
3900             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3901           }
3902         } else {
3903           // Unknown attribute
3904           cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3905         }
3906       } else {
3907         // Unknown attribute
3908         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3909       }
3910     } else {
3911       // Unknown attribute
3912       cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3913     }
3914   }
3915   _class_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3916                                             runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3917                                             runtime_invisible_annotations,
3918                                             runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3919                                             CHECK);
3920   _class_type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3921                                                  runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3922                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3923                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3924                                                  CHECK);
3925 
3926   if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute || parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3927     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_inner_classes_attribute(
3928                             cfs,
3929                             inner_classes_attribute_start,
3930                             parsed_innerclasses_attribute,
3931                             enclosing_method_class_index,
3932                             enclosing_method_method_index,
3933                             CHECK);
3934     if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute && _need_verify && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3935       guarantee_property(
3936         inner_classes_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + 4 * sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
3937         "Wrong InnerClasses attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3938     }
3939   }
3940 
3941   if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3942     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_nest_members_attribute(
3943                             cfs,
3944                             nest_members_attribute_start,
3945                             CHECK);
3946     if (_need_verify) {
3947       guarantee_property(
3948         nest_members_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
3949         "Wrong NestMembers attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3950     }
3951   }
3952 
3953   if (parsed_record_attribute) {
3954     const unsigned int calculated_attr_length = parse_classfile_record_attribute(
3955                             cfs,
3956                             cp,
3957                             record_attribute_start,
3958                             CHECK);
3959     if (_need_verify) {
3960       guarantee_property(record_attribute_length == calculated_attr_length,
3961                          "Record attribute has wrong length in class file %s",
3962                          CHECK);
3963     }
3964   }
3965 
3966   if (_max_bootstrap_specifier_index >= 0) {
3967     guarantee_property(parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute,
3968                        "Missing BootstrapMethods attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3969   }
3970 }
3971 
3972 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_attributes(InstanceKlass* k) {
3973   assert(k != NULL, "invariant");
3974 
3975   if (_synthetic_flag)
3976     k->set_is_synthetic();
3977   if (_sourcefile_index != 0) {
3978     k->set_source_file_name_index(_sourcefile_index);
3979   }
3980   if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
3981     k->set_generic_signature_index(_generic_signature_index);
3982   }
3983   if (_sde_buffer != NULL) {
3984     k->set_source_debug_extension(_sde_buffer, _sde_length);
3985   }
3986 }
3987 
3988 // Create the Annotations object that will
3989 // hold the annotations array for the Klass.
3990 void ClassFileParser::create_combined_annotations(TRAPS) {
3991     if (_class_annotations == NULL &&
3992         _class_type_annotations == NULL &&
3993         _fields_annotations == NULL &&
3994         _fields_type_annotations == NULL) {
3995       // Don't create the Annotations object unnecessarily.
3996       return;
3997     }
3998 
3999     Annotations* const annotations = Annotations::allocate(_loader_data, CHECK);
4000     annotations->set_class_annotations(_class_annotations);
4001     annotations->set_class_type_annotations(_class_type_annotations);
4002     annotations->set_fields_annotations(_fields_annotations);
4003     annotations->set_fields_type_annotations(_fields_type_annotations);
4004 
4005     // This is the Annotations object that will be
4006     // assigned to InstanceKlass being constructed.
4007     _combined_annotations = annotations;
4008 
4009     // The annotations arrays below has been transfered the
4010     // _combined_annotations so these fields can now be cleared.
4011     _class_annotations       = NULL;
4012     _class_type_annotations  = NULL;
4013     _fields_annotations      = NULL;
4014     _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
4015 }
4016 
4017 // Transfer ownership of metadata allocated to the InstanceKlass.
4018 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_metadata(
4019                                             InstanceKlass* this_klass,
4020                                             int java_fields_count,
4021                                             TRAPS) {
4022   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
4023 
4024   _cp->set_pool_holder(this_klass);
4025   this_klass->set_constants(_cp);
4026   this_klass->set_fields(_fields, java_fields_count);
4027   this_klass->set_methods(_methods);
4028   this_klass->set_inner_classes(_inner_classes);
4029   this_klass->set_nest_members(_nest_members);
4030   this_klass->set_nest_host_index(_nest_host);
4031   this_klass->set_local_interfaces(_local_interfaces);
4032   this_klass->set_annotations(_combined_annotations);
4033   this_klass->set_record_components(_record_components);
4034   // Delay the setting of _transitive_interfaces until after initialize_supers() in
4035   // fill_instance_klass(). It is because the _transitive_interfaces may be shared with
4036   // its _super. If an OOM occurs while loading the current klass, its _super field
4037   // may not have been set. When GC tries to free the klass, the _transitive_interfaces
4038   // may be deallocated mistakenly in InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(). Subsequent
4039   // dereferences to the deallocated _transitive_interfaces will result in a crash.
4040 
4041   // Clear out these fields so they don't get deallocated by the destructor
4042   clear_class_metadata();
4043 }
4044 
4045 AnnotationArray* ClassFileParser::assemble_annotations(const u1* const runtime_visible_annotations,
4046                                                        int runtime_visible_annotations_length,
4047                                                        const u1* const runtime_invisible_annotations,
4048                                                        int runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4049                                                        TRAPS) {
4050   AnnotationArray* annotations = NULL;
4051   if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL ||
4052       runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4053     annotations = MetadataFactory::new_array<u1>(_loader_data,
4054                                           runtime_visible_annotations_length +
4055                                           runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4056                                           CHECK_(annotations));
4057     if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
4058       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_visible_annotations_length; i++) {
4059         annotations->at_put(i, runtime_visible_annotations[i]);
4060       }
4061     }
4062     if (runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4063       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_invisible_annotations_length; i++) {
4064         int append = runtime_visible_annotations_length+i;
4065         annotations->at_put(append, runtime_invisible_annotations[i]);
4066       }
4067     }
4068   }
4069   return annotations;
4070 }
4071 
4072 const InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::parse_super_class(ConstantPool* const cp,
4073                                                         const int super_class_index,
4074                                                         const bool need_verify,
4075                                                         TRAPS) {
4076   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4077   const InstanceKlass* super_klass = NULL;
4078 
4079   if (super_class_index == 0) {
4080     check_property(_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()
4081                    || (_access_flags.get_flags() & JVM_ACC_VALUE),
4082                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4083                    super_class_index,
4084                    CHECK_NULL);
4085   } else {
4086     check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(super_class_index),
4087                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4088                    super_class_index,
4089                    CHECK_NULL);
4090     // The class name should be legal because it is checked when parsing constant pool.
4091     // However, make sure it is not an array type.
4092     bool is_array = false;
4093     if (cp->tag_at(super_class_index).is_klass()) {
4094       super_klass = InstanceKlass::cast(cp->resolved_klass_at(super_class_index));
4095       if (need_verify)
4096         is_array = super_klass->is_array_klass();
4097     } else if (need_verify) {
4098       is_array = (cp->klass_name_at(super_class_index)->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY);
4099     }
4100     if (need_verify) {
4101       guarantee_property(!is_array,
4102                         "Bad superclass name in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
4103     }
4104   }
4105   return super_klass;
4106 }
4107 
4108 #ifndef PRODUCT
4109 static void print_field_layout(const Symbol* name,
4110                                Array<u2>* fields,
4111                                ConstantPool* cp,
4112                                int instance_size,
4113                                int instance_fields_start,
4114                                int instance_fields_end,
4115                                int static_fields_end) {
4116 
4117   assert(name != NULL, "invariant");
4118 
4119   tty->print("%s: field layout\n", name->as_klass_external_name());
4120   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_start, "--- instance fields start ---");
4121   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4122     if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4123       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4124         fs.offset(),
4125         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4126         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4127     }
4128   }
4129   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_end, "--- instance fields end ---");
4130   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_size * wordSize, "--- instance ends ---");
4131   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields(), "--- static fields start ---");
4132   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4133     if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4134       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4135         fs.offset(),
4136         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4137         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4138     }
4139   }
4140   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", static_fields_end, "--- static fields end ---");
4141   tty->print("\n");
4142 }
4143 #endif
4144 
4145 OopMapBlocksBuilder::OopMapBlocksBuilder(unsigned int max_blocks) {
4146   _max_nonstatic_oop_maps = max_blocks;
4147   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = 0;
4148   if (max_blocks == 0) {
4149     _nonstatic_oop_maps = NULL;
4150   } else {
4151     _nonstatic_oop_maps =
4152         NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4153     memset(_nonstatic_oop_maps, 0, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * max_blocks);
4154   }
4155 }
4156 
4157 OopMapBlock* OopMapBlocksBuilder::last_oop_map() const {
4158   assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0, "Has no oop maps");
4159   return _nonstatic_oop_maps + (_nonstatic_oop_map_count - 1);
4160 }
4161 
4162 // addition of super oop maps
4163 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::initialize_inherited_blocks(OopMapBlock* blocks, unsigned int nof_blocks) {
4164   assert(nof_blocks && _nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0 &&
4165          nof_blocks <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "invariant");
4166 
4167   memcpy(_nonstatic_oop_maps, blocks, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * nof_blocks);
4168   _nonstatic_oop_map_count += nof_blocks;
4169 }
4170 
4171 // collection of oops
4172 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::add(int offset, int count) {
4173   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0) {
4174     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4175   }
4176   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4177   if (nonstatic_oop_map->count() == 0) {  // Unused map, set it up
4178     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4179     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4180   } else if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(offset)) { // contiguous, add
4181     nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(count);
4182   } else { // Need a new one...
4183     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4184     assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "range check");
4185     nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4186     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4187     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4188   }
4189 }
4190 
4191 // general purpose copy, e.g. into allocated instanceKlass
4192 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::copy(OopMapBlock* dst) {
4193   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count != 0) {
4194     memcpy(dst, _nonstatic_oop_maps, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4195   }
4196 }
4197 
4198 // Sort and compact adjacent blocks
4199 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::compact() {
4200   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= 1) {
4201     return;
4202   }
4203   /*
4204    * Since field layout sneeks in oops before values, we will be able to condense
4205    * blocks. There is potential to compact between super, own refs and values
4206    * containing refs.
4207    *
4208    * Currently compaction is slightly limited due to values being 8 byte aligned.
4209    * This may well change: FixMe if it doesn't, the code below is fairly general purpose
4210    * and maybe it doesn't need to be.
4211    */
4212   qsort(_nonstatic_oop_maps, _nonstatic_oop_map_count, sizeof(OopMapBlock),
4213         (_sort_Fn)OopMapBlock::compare_offset);
4214   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count < 2) {
4215     return;
4216   }
4217 
4218   // Make a temp copy, and iterate through and copy back into the original
4219   ResourceMark rm;
4220   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy =
4221       NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4222   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy_end = oop_maps_copy + _nonstatic_oop_map_count;
4223   copy(oop_maps_copy);
4224   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4225   unsigned int new_count = 1;
4226   oop_maps_copy++;
4227   while(oop_maps_copy < oop_maps_copy_end) {
4228     assert(nonstatic_oop_map->offset() < oop_maps_copy->offset(), "invariant");
4229     if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(oop_maps_copy->offset())) {
4230       nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4231     } else {
4232       nonstatic_oop_map++;
4233       new_count++;
4234       nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(oop_maps_copy->offset());
4235       nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4236     }
4237     oop_maps_copy++;
4238   }
4239   assert(new_count <= _nonstatic_oop_map_count, "end up with more maps after compact() ?");
4240   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = new_count;
4241 }
4242 
4243 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_on(outputStream* st) const {
4244   st->print_cr("  OopMapBlocks: %3d  /%3d", _nonstatic_oop_map_count, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4245   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
4246     OopMapBlock* map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4247     OopMapBlock* last_map = last_oop_map();
4248     assert(map <= last_map, "Last less than first");
4249     while (map <= last_map) {
4250       st->print_cr("    Offset: %3d  -%3d Count: %3d", map->offset(),
4251                    map->offset() + map->offset_span() - heapOopSize, map->count());
4252       map++;
4253     }
4254   }
4255 }
4256 
4257 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_value_on(outputStream* st) const {
4258   print_on(st);
4259 }
4260 
4261 void ClassFileParser::throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_DECL,
4262                                                 const char* msg,
4263                                                 const Symbol* name,
4264                                                 const Symbol* sig) const {
4265 
4266   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
4267   if (name == NULL || sig == NULL) {
4268     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4269         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4270         "class: %s - %s", _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4271   }
4272   else {
4273     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4274         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4275         "\"%s\" sig: \"%s\" class: %s - %s", name->as_C_string(), sig->as_C_string(),
4276         _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4277   }
4278 }
4279 
4280 // Layout fields and fill in FieldLayoutInfo.  Could use more refactoring!
4281 void ClassFileParser::layout_fields(ConstantPool* cp,
4282                                     const FieldAllocationCount* fac,
4283                                     const ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
4284                                     FieldLayoutInfo* info,
4285                                     TRAPS) {
4286 
4287   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4288 
4289   // Field size and offset computation
4290   int nonstatic_field_size = _super_klass == NULL ? 0 :
4291                                _super_klass->nonstatic_field_size();
4292   int next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = 0;
4293   int first_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = 0;
4294 
4295   // Fields that are inline types are handled differently depending if they are static or not:
4296   // - static fields are oops
4297   // - non-static fields are embedded
4298 
4299   // Count the contended fields by type.
4300   //
4301   // We ignore static fields, because @Contended is not supported for them.
4302   // The layout code below will also ignore the static fields.
4303   int nonstatic_contended_count = 0;
4304   FieldAllocationCount fac_contended;
4305   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4306     FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4307     if (fs.is_contended()) {
4308       fac_contended.count[atype]++;
4309       if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4310         nonstatic_contended_count++;
4311       }
4312     }
4313   }
4314 
4315 
4316   // Calculate the starting byte offsets
4317   int next_static_oop_offset    = InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields();
4318   // Inline types in static fields are not embedded, they are handled with oops
4319   int next_static_double_offset = next_static_oop_offset +
4320                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + fac->count[STATIC_FLATTENABLE]) * heapOopSize);
4321   if (fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) {
4322     next_static_double_offset = align_up(next_static_double_offset, BytesPerLong);
4323   }
4324 
4325   int next_static_word_offset   = next_static_double_offset +
4326                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) * BytesPerLong);
4327   int next_static_short_offset  = next_static_word_offset +
4328                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_WORD]) * BytesPerInt);
4329   int next_static_byte_offset   = next_static_short_offset +
4330                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_SHORT]) * BytesPerShort);
4331 
4332   int nonstatic_fields_start  = instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() +
4333                                 nonstatic_field_size * heapOopSize;
4334 
4335   // First field of inline types is aligned on a long boundary in order to ease
4336   // in-lining of inline types (with header removal) in packed arrays and
4337   // flatten inline types
4338   int initial_inline_type_padding = 0;
4339   if (is_inline_type()) {
4340     int old = nonstatic_fields_start;
4341     nonstatic_fields_start = align_up(nonstatic_fields_start, BytesPerLong);
4342     initial_inline_type_padding = nonstatic_fields_start - old;
4343   }
4344 
4345   int next_nonstatic_field_offset = nonstatic_fields_start;
4346 
4347   const bool is_contended_class     = parsed_annotations->is_contended();
4348 
4349   // Class is contended, pad before all the fields
4350   if (is_contended_class) {
4351     next_nonstatic_field_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4352   }
4353 
4354   // Temporary inline types restrictions
4355   if (is_inline_type()) {
4356     if (is_contended_class) {
4357       throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support @Contended annotation yet");
4358       return;
4359     }
4360   }
4361 
4362   // Compute the non-contended fields count.
4363   // The packing code below relies on these counts to determine if some field
4364   // can be squeezed into the alignment gap. Contended fields are obviously
4365   // exempt from that.
4366   unsigned int nonstatic_double_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE];
4367   unsigned int nonstatic_word_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_WORD];
4368   unsigned int nonstatic_short_count  = fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT]  - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_SHORT];
4369   unsigned int nonstatic_byte_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_BYTE];
4370   unsigned int nonstatic_oop_count    = fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP]    - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_OOP];
4371 
4372   int static_inline_type_count = 0;
4373   int nonstatic_inline_type_count = 0;
4374   int* nonstatic_inline_type_indexes = NULL;
4375   Klass** nonstatic_inline_type_klasses = NULL;
4376   unsigned int inline_type_oop_map_count = 0;
4377   int not_flattened_inline_types = 0;
4378   int not_atomic_inline_types = 0;
4379 
4380   int max_nonstatic_inline_type = fac->count[NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE] + 1;
4381 
4382   nonstatic_inline_type_indexes = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, int,
4383                                                                max_nonstatic_inline_type);
4384   for (int i = 0; i < max_nonstatic_inline_type; i++) {
4385     nonstatic_inline_type_indexes[i] = -1;
4386   }
4387   nonstatic_inline_type_klasses = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, Klass*,
4388                                                                max_nonstatic_inline_type);
4389 
4390   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, _cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4391     if (fs.allocation_type() == STATIC_FLATTENABLE) {
4392       ResourceMark rm;
4393       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4394         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4395       }
4396       static_inline_type_count++;
4397     } else if (fs.allocation_type() == NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE) {
4398       // Pre-resolve the flattenable field and check for inline type circularity issues.
4399       ResourceMark rm;
4400       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4401         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4402       }
4403       Klass* klass =
4404         SystemDictionary::resolve_flattenable_field_or_fail(&fs,
4405                                                             Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
4406                                                             _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
4407       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
4408       if (!klass->access_flags().is_inline_type()) {
4409         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError());
4410       }
4411       ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4412       // Conditions to apply flattening or not should be defined in a single place
4413       bool too_big_to_flatten = (ValueFieldMaxFlatSize >= 0 &&
4414                                  (vk->size_helper() * HeapWordSize) > ValueFieldMaxFlatSize);
4415       bool too_atomic_to_flatten = vk->is_declared_atomic();
4416       bool too_volatile_to_flatten = fs.access_flags().is_volatile();
4417       if (vk->is_naturally_atomic()) {
4418         too_atomic_to_flatten = false;
4419         //too_volatile_to_flatten = false; //FIXME
4420         // volatile fields are currently never flattened, this could change in the future
4421       }
4422       if (!(too_big_to_flatten | too_atomic_to_flatten | too_volatile_to_flatten)) {
4423         nonstatic_inline_type_indexes[nonstatic_inline_type_count] = fs.index();
4424         nonstatic_inline_type_klasses[nonstatic_inline_type_count] = klass;
4425         nonstatic_inline_type_count++;
4426 
4427         ValueKlass* vklass = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4428         if (vklass->contains_oops()) {
4429           inline_type_oop_map_count += vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4430         }
4431         fs.set_flattened(true);
4432         if (!vk->is_atomic()) {  // flat and non-atomic: take note
4433           not_atomic_inline_types++;
4434         }
4435       } else {
4436         not_flattened_inline_types++;
4437         fs.set_flattened(false);
4438       }
4439     }
4440   }
4441 
4442   // Adjusting non_static_oop_count to take into account not flattened inline types;
4443   nonstatic_oop_count += not_flattened_inline_types;
4444 
4445   // Total non-static fields count, including every contended field
4446   unsigned int nonstatic_fields_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD] +
4447                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE] +
4448                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE];
4449 
4450   const bool super_has_nonstatic_fields =
4451           (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_nonstatic_fields());
4452   const bool has_nonstatic_fields =
4453     super_has_nonstatic_fields || (nonstatic_fields_count != 0);
4454   const bool has_nonstatic_value_fields = nonstatic_inline_type_count > 0;
4455 
4456   if (is_inline_type() && (!has_nonstatic_fields)) {
4457     // There are a number of fixes required throughout the type system and JIT
4458     throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support zero instance size yet");
4459     return;
4460   }
4461 
4462   // Prepare list of oops for oop map generation.
4463   //
4464   // "offset" and "count" lists are describing the set of contiguous oop
4465   // regions. offset[i] is the start of the i-th region, which then has
4466   // count[i] oops following. Before we know how many regions are required,
4467   // we pessimistically allocate the maps to fit all the oops into the
4468   // distinct regions.
4469   //
4470   int super_oop_map_count = (_super_klass == NULL) ? 0 :_super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4471   int max_oop_map_count =
4472       super_oop_map_count +
4473       fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] +
4474       inline_type_oop_map_count +
4475       not_flattened_inline_types;
4476 
4477   OopMapBlocksBuilder* nonstatic_oop_maps = new OopMapBlocksBuilder(max_oop_map_count);
4478   if (super_oop_map_count > 0) {
4479     nonstatic_oop_maps->initialize_inherited_blocks(_super_klass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps(),
4480                                                     _super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count());
4481   }
4482 
4483   int first_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0; // will be set for first oop field
4484 
4485   bool compact_fields  = true;
4486   bool allocate_oops_first = false;
4487 
4488   // The next classes have predefined hard-coded fields offsets
4489   // (see in JavaClasses::compute_hard_coded_offsets()).
4490   // Use default fields allocation order for them.
4491   if (_loader_data->class_loader() == NULL &&
4492       (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_ref_Reference() ||
4493        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Boolean() ||
4494        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Character() ||
4495        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Float() ||
4496        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Double() ||
4497        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Byte() ||
4498        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Short() ||
4499        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Integer() ||
4500        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Long())) {
4501     allocate_oops_first = true;     // Allocate oops first
4502     compact_fields   = false; // Don't compact fields
4503   }
4504 
4505   int next_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0;
4506   int next_nonstatic_double_offset = 0;
4507 
4508   // Rearrange fields for a given allocation style
4509   if (allocate_oops_first) {
4510     // Fields order: oops, longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, padded fields
4511     next_nonstatic_oop_offset    = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4512     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset +
4513                                     (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4514   } else {
4515     // Fields order: longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, oops, padded fields
4516     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4517   }
4518 
4519   int nonstatic_oop_space_count   = 0;
4520   int nonstatic_word_space_count  = 0;
4521   int nonstatic_short_space_count = 0;
4522   int nonstatic_byte_space_count  = 0;
4523   int nonstatic_oop_space_offset = 0;
4524   int nonstatic_word_space_offset = 0;
4525   int nonstatic_short_space_offset = 0;
4526   int nonstatic_byte_space_offset = 0;
4527 
4528   // Try to squeeze some of the fields into the gaps due to
4529   // long/double alignment.
4530   if (nonstatic_double_count > 0) {
4531     int offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4532     next_nonstatic_double_offset = align_up(offset, BytesPerLong);
4533     if (compact_fields && offset != next_nonstatic_double_offset) {
4534       // Allocate available fields into the gap before double field.
4535       int length = next_nonstatic_double_offset - offset;
4536       assert(length == BytesPerInt, "");
4537       nonstatic_word_space_offset = offset;
4538       if (nonstatic_word_count > 0) {
4539         nonstatic_word_count      -= 1;
4540         nonstatic_word_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4541         length -= BytesPerInt;
4542         offset += BytesPerInt;
4543       }
4544       nonstatic_short_space_offset = offset;
4545       while (length >= BytesPerShort && nonstatic_short_count > 0) {
4546         nonstatic_short_count       -= 1;
4547         nonstatic_short_space_count += 1;
4548         length -= BytesPerShort;
4549         offset += BytesPerShort;
4550       }
4551       nonstatic_byte_space_offset = offset;
4552       while (length > 0 && nonstatic_byte_count > 0) {
4553         nonstatic_byte_count       -= 1;
4554         nonstatic_byte_space_count += 1;
4555         length -= 1;
4556       }
4557       // Allocate oop field in the gap if there are no other fields for that.
4558       nonstatic_oop_space_offset = offset;
4559       if (length >= heapOopSize && nonstatic_oop_count > 0 &&
4560           !allocate_oops_first) { // when oop fields not first
4561         nonstatic_oop_count      -= 1;
4562         nonstatic_oop_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4563         length -= heapOopSize;
4564         offset += heapOopSize;
4565       }
4566     }
4567   }
4568 
4569   int next_nonstatic_word_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset +
4570                                      (nonstatic_double_count * BytesPerLong);
4571   int next_nonstatic_short_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset +
4572                                       (nonstatic_word_count * BytesPerInt);
4573   int next_nonstatic_byte_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset +
4574                                      (nonstatic_short_count * BytesPerShort);
4575   int next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset +
4576                                        nonstatic_byte_count;
4577 
4578   // let oops jump before padding with this allocation style
4579   if (!allocate_oops_first) {
4580     next_nonstatic_oop_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4581     if( nonstatic_oop_count > 0 ) {
4582       next_nonstatic_oop_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_oop_offset, heapOopSize);
4583     }
4584     next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset + (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4585   }
4586 
4587   // Aligning embedded inline types
4588   // bug below, the current algorithm to layout embedded inline types always put them at the
4589   // end of the layout, which doesn't match the different allocation policies the VM is
4590   // supposed to provide => FixMe
4591   // Note also that the current alignment policy is to make each inline type starting on a
4592   // 64 bits boundary. This could be optimized later. For instance, it could be nice to
4593   // align inline types according to their most constrained internal type.
4594   next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4595   int next_inline_type_index = 0;
4596 
4597   // Iterate over fields again and compute correct offsets.
4598   // The field allocation type was temporarily stored in the offset slot.
4599   // oop fields are located before non-oop fields (static and non-static).
4600   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4601 
4602     // skip already laid out fields
4603     if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4604 
4605     // contended instance fields are handled below
4606     if (fs.is_contended() && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4607 
4608     int real_offset = 0;
4609     const FieldAllocationType atype = (const FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4610 
4611     // pack the rest of the fields
4612     switch (atype) {
4613       // Inline types in static fields are handled with oops
4614       case STATIC_FLATTENABLE:   // Fallthrough
4615       case STATIC_OOP:
4616         real_offset = next_static_oop_offset;
4617         next_static_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4618         break;
4619       case STATIC_BYTE:
4620         real_offset = next_static_byte_offset;
4621         next_static_byte_offset += 1;
4622         break;
4623       case STATIC_SHORT:
4624         real_offset = next_static_short_offset;
4625         next_static_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4626         break;
4627       case STATIC_WORD:
4628         real_offset = next_static_word_offset;
4629         next_static_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4630         break;
4631       case STATIC_DOUBLE:
4632         real_offset = next_static_double_offset;
4633         next_static_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4634         break;
4635       case NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE:
4636         if (fs.is_flattened()) {
4637           Klass* klass = nonstatic_inline_type_klasses[next_inline_type_index];
4638           assert(klass != NULL, "Klass should have been loaded and resolved earlier");
4639           assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(),"Must be an inline type");
4640           ValueKlass* vklass = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4641           real_offset = next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset;
4642           next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset += (vklass->size_helper()) * wordSize - vklass->first_field_offset();
4643           // aligning next inline type on a 64 bits boundary
4644           next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset, BytesPerLong);
4645           next_inline_type_index += 1;
4646 
4647           if (vklass->contains_oops()) { // add flatten oop maps
4648             int diff = real_offset - vklass->first_field_offset();
4649             const OopMapBlock* map = vklass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps();
4650             const OopMapBlock* const last_map = map + vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4651             while (map < last_map) {
4652               nonstatic_oop_maps->add(map->offset() + diff, map->count());
4653               map++;
4654             }
4655           }
4656           break;
4657         } else {
4658           // Fall through
4659         }
4660       case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4661         if( nonstatic_oop_space_count > 0 ) {
4662           real_offset = nonstatic_oop_space_offset;
4663           nonstatic_oop_space_offset += heapOopSize;
4664           nonstatic_oop_space_count  -= 1;
4665         } else {
4666           real_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset;
4667           next_nonstatic_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4668         }
4669         nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4670         break;
4671       case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4672         if( nonstatic_byte_space_count > 0 ) {
4673           real_offset = nonstatic_byte_space_offset;
4674           nonstatic_byte_space_offset += 1;
4675           nonstatic_byte_space_count  -= 1;
4676         } else {
4677           real_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset;
4678           next_nonstatic_byte_offset += 1;
4679         }
4680         break;
4681       case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4682         if( nonstatic_short_space_count > 0 ) {
4683           real_offset = nonstatic_short_space_offset;
4684           nonstatic_short_space_offset += BytesPerShort;
4685           nonstatic_short_space_count  -= 1;
4686         } else {
4687           real_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset;
4688           next_nonstatic_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4689         }
4690         break;
4691       case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4692         if( nonstatic_word_space_count > 0 ) {
4693           real_offset = nonstatic_word_space_offset;
4694           nonstatic_word_space_offset += BytesPerInt;
4695           nonstatic_word_space_count  -= 1;
4696         } else {
4697           real_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset;
4698           next_nonstatic_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4699         }
4700         break;
4701       case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4702         real_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4703         next_nonstatic_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4704         break;
4705       default:
4706         ShouldNotReachHere();
4707     }
4708     fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4709   }
4710 
4711 
4712   // Handle the contended cases.
4713   //
4714   // Each contended field should not intersect the cache line with another contended field.
4715   // In the absence of alignment information, we end up with pessimistically separating
4716   // the fields with full-width padding.
4717   //
4718   // Additionally, this should not break alignment for the fields, so we round the alignment up
4719   // for each field.
4720   if (nonstatic_contended_count > 0) {
4721 
4722     // if there is at least one contended field, we need to have pre-padding for them
4723     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4724 
4725     // collect all contended groups
4726     ResourceBitMap bm(cp->size());
4727     for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4728       // skip already laid out fields
4729       if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4730 
4731       if (fs.is_contended()) {
4732         bm.set_bit(fs.contended_group());
4733       }
4734     }
4735 
4736     int current_group = -1;
4737     while ((current_group = (int)bm.get_next_one_offset(current_group + 1)) != (int)bm.size()) {
4738 
4739       for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4740 
4741         // skip already laid out fields
4742         if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4743 
4744         // skip non-contended fields and fields from different group
4745         if (!fs.is_contended() || (fs.contended_group() != current_group)) continue;
4746 
4747         // handle statics below
4748         if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4749 
4750         int real_offset = 0;
4751         FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4752 
4753         switch (atype) {
4754           case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4755             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, 1);
4756             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4757             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += 1;
4758             break;
4759 
4760           case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4761             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerShort);
4762             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4763             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerShort;
4764             break;
4765 
4766           case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4767             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerInt);
4768             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4769             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerInt;
4770             break;
4771 
4772           case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4773             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4774             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4775             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerLong;
4776             break;
4777 
4778             // Inline types in static fields are handled with oops
4779           case NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE:
4780             throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
4781                                       "@Contended annotation not supported for inline types yet", fs.name(), fs.signature());
4782             return;
4783 
4784           case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4785             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, heapOopSize);
4786             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4787             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += heapOopSize;
4788             nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4789             break;
4790 
4791           default:
4792             ShouldNotReachHere();
4793         }
4794 
4795         if (fs.contended_group() == 0) {
4796           // Contended group defines the equivalence class over the fields:
4797           // the fields within the same contended group are not inter-padded.
4798           // The only exception is default group, which does not incur the
4799           // equivalence, and so requires intra-padding.
4800           next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4801         }
4802 
4803         fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4804       } // for
4805 
4806       // Start laying out the next group.
4807       // Note that this will effectively pad the last group in the back;
4808       // this is expected to alleviate memory contention effects for
4809       // subclass fields and/or adjacent object.
4810       // If this was the default group, the padding is already in place.
4811       if (current_group != 0) {
4812         next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4813       }
4814     }
4815 
4816     // handle static fields
4817   }
4818 
4819   // Entire class is contended, pad in the back.
4820   // This helps to alleviate memory contention effects for subclass fields
4821   // and/or adjacent object.
4822   if (is_contended_class) {
4823     assert(!is_inline_type(), "@Contended not supported for inline types yet");
4824     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4825   }
4826 
4827   int notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end;
4828   if (nonstatic_inline_type_count != 0) {
4829     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset;
4830   } else {
4831     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4832   }
4833 
4834   int nonstatic_field_sz_align = heapOopSize;
4835   if (is_inline_type()) {
4836     if ((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) > heapOopSize) {
4837       nonstatic_field_sz_align = BytesPerLong; // value copy of fields only uses jlong copy
4838     }
4839   }
4840   int nonstatic_fields_end      = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, nonstatic_field_sz_align);
4841   int instance_end              = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, wordSize);
4842   int static_fields_end         = align_up(next_static_byte_offset, wordSize);
4843 
4844   int static_field_size         = (static_fields_end -
4845                                    InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields()) / wordSize;
4846   nonstatic_field_size          = nonstatic_field_size +
4847                                   (nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) / heapOopSize;
4848 
4849   int instance_size             = align_object_size(instance_end / wordSize);
4850 
4851   assert(instance_size == align_object_size(align_up(
4852          (instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() + nonstatic_field_size*heapOopSize)
4853          + initial_inline_type_padding, wordSize) / wordSize), "consistent layout helper value");
4854 
4855 
4856   // Invariant: nonstatic_field end/start should only change if there are
4857   // nonstatic fields in the class, or if the class is contended. We compare
4858   // against the non-aligned value, so that end alignment will not fail the
4859   // assert without actually having the fields.
4860   assert((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end == nonstatic_fields_start) ||
4861          is_contended_class ||
4862          (nonstatic_fields_count > 0), "double-check nonstatic start/end");
4863 
4864   // Number of non-static oop map blocks allocated at end of klass.
4865   nonstatic_oop_maps->compact();
4866 
4867 #ifndef PRODUCT
4868   if ((PrintFieldLayout && !is_inline_type()) ||
4869       (PrintValueLayout && (is_inline_type() || has_nonstatic_value_fields))) {
4870     print_field_layout(_class_name,
4871           _fields,
4872           cp,
4873           instance_size,
4874           nonstatic_fields_start,
4875           nonstatic_fields_end,
4876           static_fields_end);
4877     nonstatic_oop_maps->print_on(tty);
4878     tty->print("\n");
4879     tty->print_cr("Instance size = %d", instance_size);
4880     tty->print_cr("Nonstatic_field_size = %d", nonstatic_field_size);
4881     tty->print_cr("Static_field_size = %d", static_field_size);
4882     tty->print_cr("Has nonstatic fields = %d", has_nonstatic_fields);
4883     tty->print_cr("---");
4884   }
4885 
4886 #endif
4887   // Pass back information needed for InstanceKlass creation
4888   info->oop_map_blocks = nonstatic_oop_maps;
4889   info->_instance_size = instance_size;
4890   info->_static_field_size = static_field_size;
4891   info->_nonstatic_field_size = nonstatic_field_size;
4892   info->_has_nonstatic_fields = has_nonstatic_fields;
4893 
4894   // An inline type is naturally atomic if it has just one field, and
4895   // that field is simple enough.
4896   info->_is_naturally_atomic = (is_inline_type() &&
4897                                 !super_has_nonstatic_fields &&
4898                                 (nonstatic_fields_count <= 1) &&
4899                                 (not_atomic_inline_types == 0) &&
4900                                 (nonstatic_contended_count == 0));
4901   // This may be too restrictive, since if all the fields fit in 64
4902   // bits we could make the decision to align instances of this class
4903   // to 64-bit boundaries, and load and store them as single words.
4904   // And on machines which supported larger atomics we could similarly
4905   // allow larger values to be atomic, if properly aligned.
4906 }
4907 
4908 void ClassFileParser::set_precomputed_flags(InstanceKlass* ik) {
4909   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
4910 
4911   const Klass* const super = ik->super();
4912 
4913   // Check if this klass has an empty finalize method (i.e. one with return bytecode only),
4914   // in which case we don't have to register objects as finalizable
4915   if (!_has_empty_finalizer) {
4916     if (_has_finalizer ||
4917         (super != NULL && super->has_finalizer())) {
4918       ik->set_has_finalizer();
4919     }
4920   }
4921 
4922 #ifdef ASSERT
4923   bool f = false;
4924   const Method* const m = ik->lookup_method(vmSymbols::finalize_method_name(),
4925                                            vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
4926   if (m != NULL && !m->is_empty_method()) {
4927       f = true;
4928   }
4929 
4930   // Spec doesn't prevent agent from redefinition of empty finalizer.
4931   // Despite the fact that it's generally bad idea and redefined finalizer
4932   // will not work as expected we shouldn't abort vm in this case
4933   if (!ik->has_redefined_this_or_super()) {
4934     assert(ik->has_finalizer() == f, "inconsistent has_finalizer");
4935   }
4936 #endif
4937 
4938   // Check if this klass supports the java.lang.Cloneable interface
4939   if (SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass_loaded()) {
4940     if (ik->is_subtype_of(SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass())) {
4941       if (ik->is_value()) {
4942         Thread *THREAD = Thread::current();
4943         throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support Cloneable");
4944         return;
4945       }
4946       ik->set_is_cloneable();
4947     }
4948   }
4949 
4950   // Check if this klass has a vanilla default constructor
4951   if (super == NULL) {
4952     // java.lang.Object has empty default constructor
4953     ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
4954   } else {
4955     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor() &&
4956         _has_vanilla_constructor) {
4957       ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
4958     }
4959 #ifdef ASSERT
4960     bool v = false;
4961     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor()) {
4962       const Method* const constructor =
4963         ik->find_method(vmSymbols::object_initializer_name(),
4964                        vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
4965       if (constructor != NULL && constructor->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
4966         v = true;
4967       }
4968     }
4969     assert(v == ik->has_vanilla_constructor(), "inconsistent has_vanilla_constructor");
4970 #endif
4971   }
4972 
4973   // If it cannot be fast-path allocated, set a bit in the layout helper.
4974   // See documentation of InstanceKlass::can_be_fastpath_allocated().
4975   assert(ik->size_helper() > 0, "layout_helper is initialized");
4976   if ((!RegisterFinalizersAtInit && ik->has_finalizer())
4977       || ik->is_abstract() || ik->is_interface()
4978       || (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Class() && ik->class_loader() == NULL)
4979       || ik->size_helper() >= FastAllocateSizeLimit) {
4980     // Forbid fast-path allocation.
4981     const jint lh = Klass::instance_layout_helper(ik->size_helper(), true);
4982     ik->set_layout_helper(lh);
4983   }
4984 }
4985 
4986 bool ClassFileParser::supports_inline_types() const {
4987   // Inline types are only supported by class file version 55 and later
4988   return _major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION;
4989 }
4990 
4991 // utility methods for appending an array with check for duplicates
4992 
4993 static void append_interfaces(GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* result,
4994                               const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const ifs) {
4995   // iterate over new interfaces
4996   for (int i = 0; i < ifs->length(); i++) {
4997     InstanceKlass* const e = ifs->at(i);
4998     assert(e->is_klass() && e->is_interface(), "just checking");
4999     // add new interface
5000     result->append_if_missing(e);
5001   }
5002 }
5003 
5004 static Array<InstanceKlass*>* compute_transitive_interfaces(const InstanceKlass* super,
5005                                                             Array<InstanceKlass*>* local_ifs,
5006                                                             ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
5007                                                             TRAPS) {
5008   assert(local_ifs != NULL, "invariant");
5009   assert(loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
5010 
5011   // Compute maximum size for transitive interfaces
5012   int max_transitive_size = 0;
5013   int super_size = 0;
5014   // Add superclass transitive interfaces size
5015   if (super != NULL) {
5016     super_size = super->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5017     max_transitive_size += super_size;
5018   }
5019   // Add local interfaces' super interfaces
5020   const int local_size = local_ifs->length();
5021   for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5022     InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5023     max_transitive_size += l->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5024   }
5025   // Finally add local interfaces
5026   max_transitive_size += local_size;
5027   // Construct array
5028   if (max_transitive_size == 0) {
5029     // no interfaces, use canonicalized array
5030     return Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
5031   } else if (max_transitive_size == super_size) {
5032     // no new local interfaces added, share superklass' transitive interface array
5033     return super->transitive_interfaces();
5034     // The three lines below are commented to work around bug JDK-8245487
5035 //  } else if (max_transitive_size == local_size) {
5036 //    // only local interfaces added, share local interface array
5037 //    return local_ifs;
5038   } else {
5039     ResourceMark rm;
5040     GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* const result = new GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>(max_transitive_size);
5041 
5042     // Copy down from superclass
5043     if (super != NULL) {
5044       append_interfaces(result, super->transitive_interfaces());
5045     }
5046 
5047     // Copy down from local interfaces' superinterfaces
5048     for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5049       InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5050       append_interfaces(result, l->transitive_interfaces());
5051     }
5052     // Finally add local interfaces
5053     append_interfaces(result, local_ifs);
5054 
5055     // length will be less than the max_transitive_size if duplicates were removed
5056     const int length = result->length();
5057     assert(length <= max_transitive_size, "just checking");
5058 
5059     if (length == 1 && result->at(0) == SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass()) {
5060       return Universe::the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array();
5061     }
5062 
5063     Array<InstanceKlass*>* const new_result =
5064       MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(loader_data, length, CHECK_NULL);
5065     for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
5066       InstanceKlass* const e = result->at(i);
5067       assert(e != NULL, "just checking");
5068       new_result->at_put(i, e);
5069     }
5070     return new_result;
5071   }
5072 }
5073 
5074 static void check_super_class_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5075   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5076   const Klass* const super = this_klass->super();
5077 
5078   if (super != NULL) {
5079 
5080     // If the loader is not the boot loader then throw an exception if its
5081     // superclass is in package jdk.internal.reflect and its loader is not a
5082     // special reflection class loader
5083     if (!this_klass->class_loader_data()->is_the_null_class_loader_data()) {
5084       assert(super->is_instance_klass(), "super is not instance klass");
5085       PackageEntry* super_package = super->package();
5086       if (super_package != NULL &&
5087           super_package->name()->fast_compare(vmSymbols::jdk_internal_reflect()) == 0 &&
5088           !java_lang_ClassLoader::is_reflection_class_loader(this_klass->class_loader())) {
5089         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5090         Exceptions::fthrow(
5091           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5092           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5093           "class %s loaded by %s cannot access jdk/internal/reflect superclass %s",
5094           this_klass->external_name(),
5095           this_klass->class_loader_data()->loader_name_and_id(),
5096           super->external_name());
5097         return;
5098       }
5099     }
5100 
5101     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5102       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, InstanceKlass::cast(super), false);
5103     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5104       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5105       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5106                                                       InstanceKlass::cast(super),
5107                                                       vca_result);
5108       if (msg == NULL) {
5109         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == super->module());
5110         Exceptions::fthrow(
5111           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5112           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5113           "class %s cannot access its %ssuperclass %s (%s%s%s)",
5114           this_klass->external_name(),
5115           super->is_abstract() ? "abstract " : "",
5116           super->external_name(),
