5117           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(super) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5118           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5119           (same_module) ? "" : super->class_in_module_of_loader());
5120       } else {
5121         // Add additional message content.
5122         Exceptions::fthrow(
5123           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5124           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5125           "superclass access check failed: %s",
5126           msg);
5127       }
5128     }
5129   }
5130 }
5131 
5132 
5133 static void check_super_interface_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5134   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5135   const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = this_klass->local_interfaces();
5136   const int lng = local_interfaces->length();
5137   for (int i = lng - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
5138     InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
5139     assert (k != NULL && k->is_interface(), "invalid interface");
5140     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5141       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, k, false);
5142     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5143       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5144       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5145                                                       k,
5146                                                       vca_result);
5147       if (msg == NULL) {
5148         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == k->module());
5149         Exceptions::fthrow(
5150           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5151           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5152           "class %s cannot access its superinterface %s (%s%s%s)",
5153           this_klass->external_name(),
5154           k->external_name(),
5155           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(k) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5156           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5157           (same_module) ? "" : k->class_in_module_of_loader());
5158       } else {
5159         // Add additional message content.
5160         Exceptions::fthrow(
5161           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5162           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5163           "superinterface check failed: %s",
5164           msg);
5165       }
5166     }
5167   }
5168 }
5169 
5170 
5171 static void check_final_method_override(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5172   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5173   const Array<Method*>* const methods = this_klass->methods();
5174   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5175 
5176   // go thru each method and check if it overrides a final method
5177   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5178     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5179 
5180     // skip private, static, and <init> methods
5181     if ((!m->is_private() && !m->is_static()) &&
5182         (m->name() != vmSymbols::object_initializer_name())) {
5183 
5184       const Symbol* const name = m->name();
5185       const Symbol* const signature = m->signature();
5186       const Klass* k = this_klass->super();
5187       const Method* super_m = NULL;
5188       while (k != NULL) {
5189         // skip supers that don't have final methods.
5190         if (k->has_final_method()) {
5191           // lookup a matching method in the super class hierarchy
5192           super_m = InstanceKlass::cast(k)->lookup_method(name, signature);
5193           if (super_m == NULL) {
5194             break; // didn't find any match; get out
5195           }
5196 
5197           if (super_m->is_final() && !super_m->is_static() &&
5198               !super_m->access_flags().is_private()) {
5199             // matching method in super is final, and not static or private
5200             bool can_access = Reflection::verify_member_access(this_klass,
5201                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5202                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5203                                                                super_m->access_flags(),
5204                                                               false, false, CHECK);
5205             if (can_access) {
5206               // this class can access super final method and therefore override
5207               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5208               Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5209                                  vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5210                                  "class %s overrides final method %s.%s%s",
5211                                  this_klass->external_name(),
5212                                  super_m->method_holder()->external_name(),
5213                                  name->as_C_string(),
5214                                  signature->as_C_string()
5215                                  );
5216               return;
5217             }
5218           }
5219 
5220           // continue to look from super_m's holder's super.
5221           k = super_m->method_holder()->super();
5222           continue;
5223         }
5224 
5225         k = k->super();
5226       }
5227     }
5228   }
5229 }
5230 
5231 
5232 // assumes that this_klass is an interface
5233 static void check_illegal_static_method(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5234   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5235   assert(this_klass->is_interface(), "not an interface");
5236   const Array<Method*>* methods = this_klass->methods();
5237   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5238 
5239   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5240     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5241     // if m is static and not the init method, throw a verify error
5242     if ((m->is_static()) && (m->name() != vmSymbols::class_initializer_name())) {
5243       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5244       Exceptions::fthrow(
5245         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5246         vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5247         "Illegal static method %s in interface %s",
5248         m->name()->as_C_string(),
5249         this_klass->external_name()
5250       );
5251       return;
5252     }
5253   }
5254 }
5255 
5256 // utility methods for format checking
5257 
5258 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_modifiers(jint flags, TRAPS) const {
5259   const bool is_module = (flags & JVM_ACC_MODULE) != 0;
5260   const bool is_inline_type = (flags & JVM_ACC_VALUE) != 0;
5261   assert(_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION || !is_module, "JVM_ACC_MODULE should not be set");
5262   assert(supports_inline_types() || !is_inline_type, "JVM_ACC_VALUE should not be set");
5263   if (is_module) {
5264     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5265     Exceptions::fthrow(
5266       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5267       vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
5268       "%s is not a class because access_flag ACC_MODULE is set",
5269       _class_name->as_C_string());
5270     return;
5271   }
5272 
5273   if (is_inline_type && !EnableValhalla) {
5274     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5275     Exceptions::fthrow(
5276       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5277       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5278       "Class modifier ACC_VALUE in class %s requires option -XX:+EnableValhalla",
5279       _class_name->as_C_string()
5280     );
5281   }
5282 
5283   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5284 
5285   const bool is_interface  = (flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE)  != 0;
5286   const bool is_abstract   = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)   != 0;
5287   const bool is_final      = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)      != 0;
5288   const bool is_super      = (flags & JVM_ACC_SUPER)      != 0;
5289   const bool is_enum       = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)       != 0;
5290   const bool is_annotation = (flags & JVM_ACC_ANNOTATION) != 0;
5291   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5292   const bool major_gte_14  = _major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION;
5293 
5294   if ((is_abstract && is_final) ||
5295       (is_interface && !is_abstract) ||
5296       (is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && (is_super || is_enum)) ||
5297       (!is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && is_annotation) ||
5298       (is_inline_type && (is_interface || is_abstract || is_enum || !is_final))) {
5299     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5300     const char* class_note = "";
5301     if (is_inline_type)  class_note = " (an inline class)";
5302     Exceptions::fthrow(
5303       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5304       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5305       "Illegal class modifiers in class %s%s: 0x%X",
5306       _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags
5307     );
5308     return;
5309   }
5310 }
5311 
5312 static bool has_illegal_visibility(jint flags) {
5313   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5314   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5315   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5316 
5317   return ((is_public && is_protected) ||
5318           (is_public && is_private) ||
5319           (is_protected && is_private));
5320 }
5321 
5322 // A legal major_version.minor_version must be one of the following:
5323 //
5324 //  Major_version >= 45 and major_version < 56, any minor_version.
5325 //  Major_version >= 56 and major_version <= JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 0.
5326 //  Major_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 65535 and --enable-preview is present.
5327 //
5328 static void verify_class_version(u2 major, u2 minor, Symbol* class_name, TRAPS){
5329   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5330   const u2 max_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION;
5331   if (major < JAVA_MIN_SUPPORTED_VERSION) {
5332     Exceptions::fthrow(
5333       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5334       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5335       "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid major version",
5336       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5337     return;
5338   }
5339 
5340   if (major > max_version) {
5341     Exceptions::fthrow(
5342       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5343       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5344       "%s has been compiled by a more recent version of the Java Runtime (class file version %u.%u), "
5345       "this version of the Java Runtime only recognizes class file versions up to %u.0",
5346       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
5347     return;
5348   }
5349 
5350   if (major < JAVA_12_VERSION || minor == 0) {
5351     return;
5352   }
5353 
5354   if (minor == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION) {
5355     if (major != max_version) {
5356       Exceptions::fthrow(
5357         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5358         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5359         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with preview features that are unsupported. "
5360         "This version of the Java Runtime only recognizes preview features for class file version %u.%u",
5361         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION, JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION);
5362       return;
5363     }
5364 
5365     if (!Arguments::enable_preview()) {
5366       Exceptions::fthrow(
5367         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5368         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5369         "Preview features are not enabled for %s (class file version %u.%u). Try running with '--enable-preview'",
5370         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5371       return;
5372     }
5373 
5374   } else { // minor != JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION
5375     Exceptions::fthrow(
5376         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5377         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5378         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid non-zero minor version",
5379         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5380   }
5381 }
5382 
5383 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_modifiers(jint flags,
5384                                                    bool is_interface,
5385                                                    bool is_inline_type,
5386                                                    TRAPS) const {
5387   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5388 
5389   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5390   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5391   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5392   const bool is_static    = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)    != 0;
5393   const bool is_final     = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)     != 0;
5394   const bool is_volatile  = (flags & JVM_ACC_VOLATILE)  != 0;
5395   const bool is_transient = (flags & JVM_ACC_TRANSIENT) != 0;
5396   const bool is_enum      = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)      != 0;
5397   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5398 
5399   bool is_illegal = false;
5400 
5401   if (is_interface) {
5402     if (!is_public || !is_static || !is_final || is_private ||
5403         is_protected || is_volatile || is_transient ||
5404         (major_gte_1_5 && is_enum)) {
5405       is_illegal = true;
5406     }
5407   } else { // not interface
5408     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags) || (is_final && is_volatile)) {
5409       is_illegal = true;
5410     } else {
5411       if (is_inline_type && !is_static && !is_final) {
5412         is_illegal = true;
5413       }
5414     }
5415   }
5416 
5417   if (is_illegal) {
5418     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5419     Exceptions::fthrow(
5420       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5421       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5422       "Illegal field modifiers in class %s: 0x%X",
5423       _class_name->as_C_string(), flags);
5424     return;
5425   }
5426 }
5427 
5428 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_modifiers(jint flags,
5429                                                     bool is_interface,
5430                                                     bool is_inline_type,
5431                                                     const Symbol* name,
5432                                                     TRAPS) const {
5433   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5434 
5435   const bool is_public       = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)       != 0;
5436   const bool is_private      = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)      != 0;
5437   const bool is_static       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)       != 0;
5438   const bool is_final        = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)        != 0;
5439   const bool is_native       = (flags & JVM_ACC_NATIVE)       != 0;
5440   const bool is_abstract     = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)     != 0;
5441   const bool is_bridge       = (flags & JVM_ACC_BRIDGE)       != 0;
5442   const bool is_strict       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STRICT)       != 0;
5443   const bool is_synchronized = (flags & JVM_ACC_SYNCHRONIZED) != 0;
5444   const bool is_protected    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED)    != 0;
5445   const bool major_gte_1_5   = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5446   const bool major_gte_8     = _major_version >= JAVA_8_VERSION;
5447   const bool is_initializer  = (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name());
5448 
5449   bool is_illegal = false;
5450 
5451   const char* class_note = "";
5452 
5453   if (is_interface) {
5454     if (major_gte_8) {
5455       // Class file version is JAVA_8_VERSION or later Methods of
5456       // interfaces may set any of the flags except ACC_PROTECTED,
5457       // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, and ACC_SYNCHRONIZED; they must
5458       // have exactly one of the ACC_PUBLIC or ACC_PRIVATE flags set.
5459       if ((is_public == is_private) || /* Only one of private and public should be true - XNOR */
5460           (is_native || is_protected || is_final || is_synchronized) ||
5461           // If a specific method of a class or interface has its
5462           // ACC_ABSTRACT flag set, it must not have any of its
5463           // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, ACC_PRIVATE, ACC_STATIC,
5464           // ACC_STRICT, or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED flags set.  No need to
5465           // check for ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED as
5466           // those flags are illegal irrespective of ACC_ABSTRACT being set or not.
5467           (is_abstract && (is_private || is_static || is_strict))) {
5468         is_illegal = true;
5469       }
5470     } else if (major_gte_1_5) {
5471       // Class file version in the interval [JAVA_1_5_VERSION, JAVA_8_VERSION)
5472       if (!is_public || is_private || is_protected || is_static || is_final ||
5473           is_synchronized || is_native || !is_abstract || is_strict) {
5474         is_illegal = true;
5475       }
5476     } else {
5477       // Class file version is pre-JAVA_1_5_VERSION
5478       if (!is_public || is_static || is_final || is_native || !is_abstract) {
5479         is_illegal = true;
5480       }
5481     }
5482   } else { // not interface
5483     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags)) {
5484       is_illegal = true;
5485     } else {
5486       if (is_initializer) {
5487         if (is_final || is_synchronized || is_native ||
5488             is_abstract || (major_gte_1_5 && is_bridge)) {
5489           is_illegal = true;
5490         }
5491         if (!is_static && !is_inline_type) {
5492           // OK, an object constructor in a regular class
5493         } else if (is_static && is_inline_type) {
5494           // OK, a static init factory in an inline class
5495         } else {
5496           // but no other combinations are allowed
5497           is_illegal = true;
5498           class_note = (is_inline_type ? " (an inline class)" : " (not an inline class)");
5499         }
5500       } else { // not initializer
5501         if (is_inline_type && is_synchronized && !is_static) {
5502           is_illegal = true;
5503           class_note = " (an inline class)";
5504         } else {
5505           if (is_abstract) {
5506             if ((is_final || is_native || is_private || is_static ||
5507                 (major_gte_1_5 && (is_synchronized || is_strict)))) {
5508               is_illegal = true;
5509             }
5510           }
5511         }
5512       }
5513     }
5514   }
5515 
5516   if (is_illegal) {
5517     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5518     Exceptions::fthrow(
5519       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5520       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5521       "Method %s in class %s%s has illegal modifiers: 0x%X",
5522       name->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags);
5523     return;
5524   }
5525 }
5526 
5527 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_utf8(const unsigned char* buffer,
5528                                         int length,
5529                                         TRAPS) const {
5530   assert(_need_verify, "only called when _need_verify is true");
5531   if (!UTF8::is_legal_utf8(buffer, length, _major_version <= 47)) {
5532     classfile_parse_error("Illegal UTF8 string in constant pool in class file %s", CHECK);
5533   }
5534 }
5535 
5536 // Unqualified names may not contain the characters '.', ';', '[', or '/'.
5537 // In class names, '/' separates unqualified names.  This is verified in this function also.
5538 // Method names also may not contain the characters '<' or '>', unless <init>
5539 // or <clinit>.  Note that method names may not be <init> or <clinit> in this
5540 // method.  Because these names have been checked as special cases before
5541 // calling this method in verify_legal_method_name.
5542 //
5543 // This method is also called from the modular system APIs in modules.cpp
5544 // to verify the validity of module and package names.
5545 bool ClassFileParser::verify_unqualified_name(const char* name,
5546                                               unsigned int length,
5547                                               int type) {
5548   if (length == 0) return false;  // Must have at least one char.
5549   for (const char* p = name; p != name + length; p++) {
5550     switch(*p) {
5551       case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT:
5552       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS:
5553       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5554         // do not permit '.', ';', or '['
5555         return false;
5556       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH:
5557         // check for '//' or leading or trailing '/' which are not legal
5558         // unqualified name must not be empty
5559         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalClass) {
5560           if (p == name || p+1 >= name+length ||
5561               *(p+1) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5562             return false;
5563           }
5564         } else {
5565           return false;   // do not permit '/' unless it's class name
5566         }
5567         break;
5568       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL:
5569       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDSPECIAL:
5570         // do not permit '<' or '>' in method names
5571         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalMethod) {
5572           return false;
5573         }
5574     }
5575   }
5576   return true;
5577 }
5578 
5579 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5580 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5581 // be taken as a fieldname. Allow '/' if slash_ok is true.
5582 // Return a pointer to just past the fieldname.
5583 // Return NULL if no fieldname at all was found, or in the case of slash_ok
5584 // being true, we saw consecutive slashes (meaning we were looking for a
5585 // qualified path but found something that was badly-formed).
5586 static const char* skip_over_field_name(const char* const name,
5587                                         bool slash_ok,
5588                                         unsigned int length) {
5589   const char* p;
5590   jboolean last_is_slash = false;
5591   jboolean not_first_ch = false;
5592 
5593   for (p = name; p != name + length; not_first_ch = true) {
5594     const char* old_p = p;
5595     jchar ch = *p;
5596     if (ch < 128) {
5597       p++;
5598       // quick check for ascii
5599       if ((ch >= 'a' && ch <= 'z') ||
5600         (ch >= 'A' && ch <= 'Z') ||
5601         (ch == '_' || ch == '$') ||
5602         (not_first_ch && ch >= '0' && ch <= '9')) {
5603         last_is_slash = false;
5604         continue;
5605       }
5606       if (slash_ok && ch == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5607         if (last_is_slash) {
5608           return NULL;  // Don't permit consecutive slashes
5609         }
5610         last_is_slash = true;
5611         continue;
5612       }
5613     }
5614     else {
5615       jint unicode_ch;
5616       char* tmp_p = UTF8::next_character(p, &unicode_ch);
5617       p = tmp_p;
5618       last_is_slash = false;
5619       // Check if ch is Java identifier start or is Java identifier part
5620       // 4672820: call java.lang.Character methods directly without generating separate tables.
5621       EXCEPTION_MARK;
5622       // return value
5623       JavaValue result(T_BOOLEAN);
5624       // Set up the arguments to isJavaIdentifierStart or isJavaIdentifierPart
5625       JavaCallArguments args;
5626       args.push_int(unicode_ch);
5627 
5628       if (not_first_ch) {
5629         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierPart(char ch);
5630         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5631           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5632           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierPart_name(),
5633           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5634           &args,
5635           THREAD);
5636       } else {
5637         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierStart(char ch);
5638         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5639           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5640           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierStart_name(),
5641           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5642           &args,
5643           THREAD);
5644       }
5645       if (HAS_PENDING_EXCEPTION) {
5646         CLEAR_PENDING_EXCEPTION;
5647         return NULL;
5648       }
5649       if(result.get_jboolean()) {
5650         continue;
5651       }
5652     }
5653     return (not_first_ch) ? old_p : NULL;
5654   }
5655   return (not_first_ch) ? p : NULL;
5656 }
5657 
5658 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5659 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5660 // be taken as a field signature. Allow "void" if void_ok.
5661 // Return a pointer to just past the signature.
5662 // Return NULL if no legal signature is found.
5663 const char* ClassFileParser::skip_over_field_signature(const char* signature,
5664                                                        bool void_ok,
5665                                                        unsigned int length,
5666                                                        TRAPS) const {
5667   unsigned int array_dim = 0;
5668   while (length > 0) {
5669     switch (signature[0]) {
5670     case JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID: if (!void_ok) { return NULL; }
5671     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BOOLEAN:
5672     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BYTE:
5673     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CHAR:
5674     case JVM_SIGNATURE_SHORT:
5675     case JVM_SIGNATURE_INT:
5676     case JVM_SIGNATURE_FLOAT:
5677     case JVM_SIGNATURE_LONG:
5678     case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOUBLE:
5679       return signature + 1;
5680     case JVM_SIGNATURE_VALUETYPE:
5681       // Can't enable this check until JDK upgrades the bytecode generators
5682       // if (_major_version < CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS ) {
5683       //   classfile_parse_error("Class name contains illegal Q-signature "
5684       //                                    "in descriptor in class file %s",
5685       //                                    CHECK_0);
5686       // }
5687       // fall through
5688     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CLASS:
5689     {
5690       if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5691         // Skip over the class name if one is there
5692         const char* const p = skip_over_field_name(signature + 1, true, --length);
5693 
5694         // The next character better be a semicolon
5695         if (p && (p - signature) > 1 && p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS) {
5696           return p + 1;
5697         }
5698       }
5699       else {
5700         // Skip leading 'L' or 'Q' and ignore first appearance of ';'
5701         signature++;
5702         const char* c = (const char*) memchr(signature, JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS, length - 1);
5703         // Format check signature
5704         if (c != NULL) {
5705           int newlen = c - (char*) signature;
5706           bool legal = verify_unqualified_name(signature, newlen, LegalClass);
5707           if (!legal) {
5708             classfile_parse_error("Class name is empty or contains illegal character "
5709                                   "in descriptor in class file %s",
5710                                   CHECK_NULL);
5711             return NULL;
5712           }
5713           return signature + newlen + 1;
5714         }
5715       }
5716       return NULL;
5717     }
5718     case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5719       array_dim++;
5720       if (array_dim > 255) {
5721         // 4277370: array descriptor is valid only if it represents 255 or fewer dimensions.
5722         classfile_parse_error("Array type descriptor has more than 255 dimensions in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
5723       }
5724       // The rest of what's there better be a legal signature
5725       signature++;
5726       length--;
5727       void_ok = false;
5728       break;
5729     default:
5730       return NULL;
5731     }
5732   }
5733   return NULL;
5734 }
5735 
5736 // Checks if name is a legal class name.
5737 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5738   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5739 
5740   assert(name->refcount() > 0, "symbol must be kept alive");
5741   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5742   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5743   bool legal = false;
5744 
5745   if (length > 0) {
5746     const char* p;
5747     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY) {
5748       p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5749       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5750     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5751       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5752         p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, true, length);
5753         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5754       }
5755     } else if (_major_version >= CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS && bytes[length - 1] == ';' ) {
5756       // Support for L...; and Q...; descriptors
5757       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes + 1, length - 2, LegalClass);
5758     } else {
5759       // 4900761: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5760       // Class names may be drawn from the entire Unicode character set.
5761       // Identifiers between '/' must be unqualified names.
5762       // The utf8 string has been verified when parsing cpool entries.
5763       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalClass);
5764     }
5765   }
5766   if (!legal) {
5767     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5768     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5769     Exceptions::fthrow(
5770       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5771       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5772       "Illegal class name \"%.*s\" in class file %s", length, bytes,
5773       _class_name->as_C_string()
5774     );
5775     return;
5776   }
5777 }
5778 
5779 // Checks if name is a legal field name.
5780 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5781   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5782 
5783   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5784   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5785   bool legal = false;
5786 
5787   if (length > 0) {
5788     if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5789       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5790         const char* p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5791         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5792       }
5793     } else {
5794       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5795       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalField);
5796     }
5797   }
5798 
5799   if (!legal) {
5800     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5801     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5802     Exceptions::fthrow(
5803       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5804       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5805       "Illegal field name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5806       _class_name->as_C_string()
5807     );
5808     return;
5809   }
5810 }
5811 
5812 // Checks if name is a legal method name.
5813 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5814   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5815 
5816   assert(name != NULL, "method name is null");
5817   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5818   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5819   bool legal = false;
5820 
5821   if (length > 0) {
5822     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5823       if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name() || name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name()) {
5824         legal = true;
5825       }
5826     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5827       const char* p;
5828       p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5829       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5830     } else {
5831       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5832       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalMethod);
5833     }
5834   }
5835 
5836   if (!legal) {
5837     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5838     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5839     Exceptions::fthrow(
5840       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5841       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5842       "Illegal method name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5843       _class_name->as_C_string()
5844     );
5845     return;
5846   }
5847 }
5848 
5849 
5850 // Checks if signature is a legal field signature.
5851 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_signature(const Symbol* name,
5852                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5853                                                    TRAPS) const {
5854   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5855 
5856   const char* const bytes = (const char* const)signature->bytes();
5857   const unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5858   const char* const p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5859 
5860   if (p == NULL || (p - bytes) != (int)length) {
5861     throwIllegalSignature("Field", name, signature, CHECK);
5862   }
5863 }
5864 
5865 // Checks if signature is a legal method signature.
5866 // Returns number of parameters
5867 int ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_signature(const Symbol* name,
5868                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5869                                                    TRAPS) const {
5870   if (!_need_verify) {
5871     // make sure caller's args_size will be less than 0 even for non-static
5872     // method so it will be recomputed in compute_size_of_parameters().
5873     return -2;
5874   }
5875 
5876   // Class initializers cannot have args for class format version >= 51.
5877   if (name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name() &&
5878       signature != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() &&
5879       _major_version >= JAVA_7_VERSION) {
5880     throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
5881     return 0;
5882   }
5883 
5884   unsigned int args_size = 0;
5885   const char* p = (const char*)signature->bytes();
5886   unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5887   const char* nextp;
5888 
5889   // The first character must be a '('
5890   if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_FUNC)) {
5891     length--;
5892     // Skip over legal field signatures
5893     nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5894     while ((length > 0) && (nextp != NULL)) {
5895       args_size++;
5896       if (p[0] == 'J' || p[0] == 'D') {
5897         args_size++;
5898       }
5899       length -= nextp - p;
5900       p = nextp;
5901       nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5902     }
5903     // The first non-signature thing better be a ')'
5904     if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDFUNC)) {
5905       length--;
5906       if (name->utf8_length() > 0 && name->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5907         // All constructor methods must return void
5908         if ((length == 1) && (p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID)) {
5909           return args_size;
5910         }
5911         // All static init methods must return the current class
5912         if ((length >= 3) && (p[length-1] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS)
5913             && name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
5914           nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
5915           if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
5916             // The actual class will be checked against current class
5917             // when the method is defined (see parse_method).
5918             // A reference to a static init with a bad return type
5919             // will load and verify OK, but will fail to link.
5920             return args_size;
5921           }
5922         }
5923         // The distinction between static factory methods and
5924         // constructors depends on the JVM_ACC_STATIC modifier.
5925         // This distinction must be reflected in a void or non-void
5926         // return. For declared methods, the check is in parse_method.
5927       } else {
5928         // Now we better just have a return value
5929         nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
5930         if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
5931           return args_size;
5932         }
5933       }
5934     }
5935   }
5936   // Report error
5937   throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
5938   return 0;
5939 }
5940 
5941 int ClassFileParser::static_field_size() const {
5942   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5943   return _field_info->_static_field_size;
5944 }

5946 int ClassFileParser::total_oop_map_count() const {
5947   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5948   return _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count;
5949 }

5951 jint ClassFileParser::layout_size() const {
5952   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5953   return _field_info->_instance_size;
5954 }
5955 
5956 static void check_methods_for_intrinsics(const InstanceKlass* ik,
5957                                          const Array<Method*>* methods) {
5958   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
5959   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
5960 
5961   // Set up Method*::intrinsic_id as soon as we know the names of methods.
5962   // (We used to do this lazily, but now we query it in Rewriter,
5963   // which is eagerly done for every method, so we might as well do it now,
5964   // when everything is fresh in memory.)
5965   const vmSymbols::SID klass_id = Method::klass_id_for_intrinsics(ik);
5966 
5967   if (klass_id != vmSymbols::NO_SID) {
5968     for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
5969       Method* method = methods->at(j);
5970       method->init_intrinsic_id();
5971 
5972       if (CheckIntrinsics) {
5973         // Check if an intrinsic is defined for method 'method',
5974         // but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.
5975         if (method->intrinsic_id() != vmIntrinsics::_none &&
5976             !method->intrinsic_candidate()) {
5977               tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
5978               "but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.%s",
5979               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
5980               NOT_DEBUG(" Method will not be inlined.") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
5981             );
5982           tty->cr();
5983           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
5984         }
5985         // Check is the method 'method' is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate,
5986         // but there is no intrinsic available for it.
5987         if (method->intrinsic_candidate() &&
5988           method->intrinsic_id() == vmIntrinsics::_none) {
5989             tty->print("Method [%s] is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate, "
5990               "but no compiler intrinsic is defined for the method.%s",
5991               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
5992               NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
5993             );
5994           tty->cr();
5995           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
5996         }
5997       }
5998     } // end for
5999 
6000 #ifdef ASSERT
6001     if (CheckIntrinsics) {
6002       // Check for orphan methods in the current class. A method m
6003       // of a class C is orphan if an intrinsic is defined for method m,
6004       // but class C does not declare m.
6005       // The check is potentially expensive, therefore it is available
6006       // only in debug builds.
6007 
6008       for (int id = vmIntrinsics::FIRST_ID; id < (int)vmIntrinsics::ID_LIMIT; ++id) {
6009         if (vmIntrinsics::_compiledLambdaForm == id) {
6010           // The _compiledLamdbdaForm intrinsic is a special marker for bytecode
6011           // generated for the JVM from a LambdaForm and therefore no method
6012           // is defined for it.
6013           continue;
6014         }
6015 
6016         if (vmIntrinsics::class_for(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id)) == klass_id) {
6017           // Check if the current class contains a method with the same
6018           // name, flags, signature.
6019           bool match = false;
6020           for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
6021             const Method* method = methods->at(j);
6022             if (method->intrinsic_id() == id) {
6023               match = true;
6024               break;
6025             }
6026           }
6027 
6028           if (!match) {
6029             char buf[1000];
6030             tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
6031                        "but the method is not available in class [%s].%s",
6032                         vmIntrinsics::short_name_as_C_string(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id),
6033                                                              buf, sizeof(buf)),
6034                         ik->name()->as_C_string(),
6035                         NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6036             );
6037             tty->cr();
6038             DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6039           }
6040         }
6041       } // end for
6042     } // CheckIntrinsics
6043 #endif // ASSERT
6044   }
6045 }
6046 
6047 // Called from a factory method in KlassFactory, not from this file.
6048 InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::create_instance_klass(bool changed_by_loadhook, TRAPS) {
6049   if (_klass != NULL) {
6050     return _klass;
6051   }
6052 
6053   InstanceKlass* const ik =
6054     InstanceKlass::allocate_instance_klass(*this, CHECK_NULL);
6055 
6056   fill_instance_klass(ik, changed_by_loadhook, CHECK_NULL);
6057   assert(_klass == ik, "invariant");
6058 
6059 
6060   if (ik->should_store_fingerprint()) {
6061     ik->store_fingerprint(_stream->compute_fingerprint());
6062   }
6063 
6064   ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(false);
6065   if (UseAOT && ik->supers_have_passed_fingerprint_checks()) {
6066     uint64_t aot_fp = AOTLoader::get_saved_fingerprint(ik);
6067     uint64_t fp = ik->has_stored_fingerprint() ? ik->get_stored_fingerprint() : _stream->compute_fingerprint();
6068     if (aot_fp != 0 && aot_fp == fp) {
6069       // This class matches with a class saved in an AOT library
6070       ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(true);
6071     } else {
6072       ResourceMark rm;
6073       log_info(class, fingerprint)("%s :  expected = " PTR64_FORMAT " actual = " PTR64_FORMAT,
6074                                  ik->external_name(), aot_fp, _stream->compute_fingerprint());
6075     }
6076   }
6077 
6078   if (ik->is_value()) {
6079     ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(ik);
6080     oop val = ik->allocate_instance(CHECK_NULL);
6081     vk->set_default_value(val);
6082   }
6083 
6084   return ik;
6085 }
6086 
6087 // Return true if the specified class is not a valid super class for an inline type.
6088 // A valid super class for an inline type is abstract, has no instance fields,
6089 // does not implement interface java.lang.IdentityObject (checked elsewhere), has
6090 // an empty body-less no-arg constructor, and no synchronized instance methods.
6091 // This function doesn't check if the class's super types are invalid.  Those checks
6092 // are done elsewhere.  The final determination of whether or not a class is an
6093 // invalid super type for an inline class is done in fill_instance_klass().
6094 bool ClassFileParser::is_invalid_super_for_inline_type() {
6095   if (class_name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6096     return true;
6097   }
6098   if (is_interface() || class_name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
6099     return false;
6100   }
6101   if (!access_flags().is_abstract() || _has_nonstatic_fields) {
6102     return true;
6103   } else {
6104     // Look at each method
6105     for (int x = 0; x < _methods->length(); x++) {
6106       const Method* const method = _methods->at(x);
6107       if (method->is_synchronized() && !method->is_static()) {
6108         return true;
6109 
6110       } else if (method->name() == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
6111         if (method->signature() != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() ||
6112             !method->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
6113           return true;
6114         }
6115       }
6116     }
6117   }
6118   return false;
6119 }
6120 
6121 void ClassFileParser::fill_instance_klass(InstanceKlass* ik, bool changed_by_loadhook, TRAPS) {
6122   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
6123 
6124   // Set name and CLD before adding to CLD
6125   ik->set_class_loader_data(_loader_data);
6126   ik->set_name(_class_name);
6127 
6128   // Add all classes to our internal class loader list here,
6129   // including classes in the bootstrap (NULL) class loader.
6130   const bool publicize = !is_internal();
6131 
6132   _loader_data->add_class(ik, publicize);
6133 
6134   set_klass_to_deallocate(ik);
6135 
6136   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6137   assert(ik->static_field_size() == _field_info->_static_field_size, "sanity");
6138   assert(ik->nonstatic_oop_map_count() == _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count,
6139          "sanity");
6140 
6141   assert(ik->is_instance_klass(), "sanity");
6142   assert(ik->size_helper() == _field_info->_instance_size, "sanity");
6143 
6144   // Fill in information already parsed
6145   ik->set_should_verify_class(_need_verify);
6146 
6147   // Not yet: supers are done below to support the new subtype-checking fields
6148   ik->set_nonstatic_field_size(_field_info->_nonstatic_field_size);
6149   ik->set_has_nonstatic_fields(_field_info->_has_nonstatic_fields);
6150   if (_field_info->_is_naturally_atomic && ik->is_value()) {
6151     ik->set_is_naturally_atomic();
6152   }
6153   if (_is_empty_inline_type) {
6154     ik->set_is_empty_inline_type();
6155   }
6156 
6157   if (this->_invalid_inline_super) {
6158     ik->set_invalid_inline_super();
6159   }
6160 
6161   if (_has_injected_identityObject) {
6162     ik->set_has_injected_identityObject();
6163   }
6164 
6165   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
6166   ik->set_static_oop_field_count(_fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + _fac->count[STATIC_FLATTENABLE]);
6167 
6168   // this transfers ownership of a lot of arrays from
6169   // the parser onto the InstanceKlass*
6170   apply_parsed_class_metadata(ik, _java_fields_count, CHECK);
6171 
6172   // note that is not safe to use the fields in the parser from this point on
6173   assert(NULL == _cp, "invariant");
6174   assert(NULL == _fields, "invariant");
6175   assert(NULL == _methods, "invariant");
6176   assert(NULL == _inner_classes, "invariant");
6177   assert(NULL == _nest_members, "invariant");
6178   assert(NULL == _local_interfaces, "invariant");
6179   assert(NULL == _combined_annotations, "invariant");
6180   assert(NULL == _record_components, "invariant");
6181 
6182   if (_has_final_method) {
6183     ik->set_has_final_method();
6184   }
6185 
6186   ik->copy_method_ordering(_method_ordering, CHECK);
6187   // The InstanceKlass::_methods_jmethod_ids cache
6188   // is managed on the assumption that the initial cache
6189   // size is equal to the number of methods in the class. If
6190   // that changes, then InstanceKlass::idnum_can_increment()
6191   // has to be changed accordingly.
6192   ik->set_initial_method_idnum(ik->methods()->length());
6193 
6194   ik->set_this_class_index(_this_class_index);
6195 
6196   if (is_unsafe_anonymous()) {
6197     // _this_class_index is a CONSTANT_Class entry that refers to this
6198     // anonymous class itself. If this class needs to refer to its own methods or
6199     // fields, it would use a CONSTANT_MethodRef, etc, which would reference
6200     // _this_class_index. However, because this class is anonymous (it's
6201     // not stored in SystemDictionary), _this_class_index cannot be resolved
6202     // with ConstantPool::klass_at_impl, which does a SystemDictionary lookup.
6203     // Therefore, we must eagerly resolve _this_class_index now.
6204     ik->constants()->klass_at_put(_this_class_index, ik);
6205   }
6206 
6207   ik->set_minor_version(_minor_version);
6208   ik->set_major_version(_major_version);
6209   ik->set_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6210   ik->set_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6211   if (_is_declared_atomic) {
6212     ik->set_is_declared_atomic();
6213   }
6214 
6215   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6216     assert (ik->is_unsafe_anonymous(), "should be the same");
6217     ik->set_unsafe_anonymous_host(_unsafe_anonymous_host);
6218   }
6219 
6220   // Set PackageEntry for this_klass
6221   oop cl = ik->class_loader();
6222   Handle clh = Handle(THREAD, java_lang_ClassLoader::non_reflection_class_loader(cl));
6223   ClassLoaderData* cld = ClassLoaderData::class_loader_data_or_null(clh());
6224   ik->set_package(cld, NULL, CHECK);
6225 
6226   const Array<Method*>* const methods = ik->methods();
6227   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
6228   const int methods_len = methods->length();
6229 
6230   check_methods_for_intrinsics(ik, methods);
6231 
6232   // Fill in field values obtained by parse_classfile_attributes
6233   if (_parsed_annotations->has_any_annotations()) {
6234     _parsed_annotations->apply_to(ik);
6235   }
6236 
6237   apply_parsed_class_attributes(ik);
6238 
6239   // Miranda methods
6240   if ((_num_miranda_methods > 0) ||
6241       // if this class introduced new miranda methods or
6242       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_miranda_methods())
6243         // super class exists and this class inherited miranda methods
6244      ) {
6245        ik->set_has_miranda_methods(); // then set a flag
6246   }
6247 
6248   // Fill in information needed to compute superclasses.
6249   ik->initialize_supers(const_cast<InstanceKlass*>(_super_klass), _transitive_interfaces, CHECK);
6250   ik->set_transitive_interfaces(_transitive_interfaces);
6251   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6252 
6253   // Initialize itable offset tables
6254   klassItable::setup_itable_offset_table(ik);
6255 
6256   // Compute transitive closure of interfaces this class implements
6257   // Do final class setup
6258   OopMapBlocksBuilder* oop_map_blocks = _field_info->oop_map_blocks;
6259   if (oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
6260     oop_map_blocks->copy(ik->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps());
6261   }
6262 
6263   if (_has_contended_fields || _parsed_annotations->is_contended() ||
6264       ( _super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_contended_annotations())) {
6265     ik->set_has_contended_annotations(true);
6266   }
6267 
6268   // Fill in has_finalizer, has_vanilla_constructor, and layout_helper
6269   set_precomputed_flags(ik);
6270 
6271   // check if this class can access its super class
6272   check_super_class_access(ik, CHECK);
6273 
6274   // check if this class can access its superinterfaces
6275   check_super_interface_access(ik, CHECK);
6276 
6277   // check if this class overrides any final method
6278   check_final_method_override(ik, CHECK);
6279 
6280   // reject static interface methods prior to Java 8
6281   if (ik->is_interface() && _major_version < JAVA_8_VERSION) {
6282     check_illegal_static_method(ik, CHECK);
6283   }
6284 
6285   // Obtain this_klass' module entry
6286   ModuleEntry* module_entry = ik->module();
6287   assert(module_entry != NULL, "module_entry should always be set");
6288 
6289   // Obtain java.lang.Module
6290   Handle module_handle(THREAD, module_entry->module());
6291 
6292   // Allocate mirror and initialize static fields
6293   // The create_mirror() call will also call compute_modifiers()
6294   java_lang_Class::create_mirror(ik,
6295                                  Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
6296                                  module_handle,
6297                                  _protection_domain,
6298                                  CHECK);
6299 
6300   assert(_all_mirandas != NULL, "invariant");
6301 
6302   // Generate any default methods - default methods are public interface methods
6303   // that have a default implementation.  This is new with Java 8.
6304   if (_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
6305     DefaultMethods::generate_default_methods(ik,
6306                                              _all_mirandas,
6307                                              CHECK);
6308   }
6309 
6310   // Add read edges to the unnamed modules of the bootstrap and app class loaders.
6311   if (changed_by_loadhook && !module_handle.is_null() && module_entry->is_named() &&
6312       !module_entry->has_default_read_edges()) {
6313     if (!module_entry->set_has_default_read_edges()) {
6314       // We won a potential race
6315       JvmtiExport::add_default_read_edges(module_handle, THREAD);
6316     }
6317   }
6318 
6319   int nfields = ik->java_fields_count();
6320   if (ik->is_value()) nfields++;
6321   for (int i = 0; i < nfields; i++) {
6322     if (ik->field_is_flattenable(i)) {
6323       Symbol* klass_name = ik->field_signature(i)->fundamental_name(CHECK);
6324       // Inline classes for instance fields must have been pre-loaded
6325       // Inline classes for static fields might not have been loaded yet
6326       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::find(klass_name,
6327           Handle(THREAD, ik->class_loader()),
6328           Handle(THREAD, ik->protection_domain()), CHECK);
6329       if (klass != NULL) {
6330         assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(), "Inline type expected");
6331         ik->set_value_field_klass(i, klass);
6332       }
6333       klass_name->decrement_refcount();
6334     } else
6335       if (is_inline_type() && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_FIELD_INTERNAL) != 0)
6336         && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_STATIC) != 0)) {
6337       ValueKlass::cast(ik)->set_default_value_offset(ik->field_offset(i));
6338     }
6339   }
6340 
6341   if (is_inline_type()) {
6342     ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(ik);
6343     if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
6344       vk->set_alignment(_alignment);
6345       vk->set_first_field_offset(_first_field_offset);
6346       vk->set_exact_size_in_bytes(_exact_size_in_bytes);
6347     } else {
6348       vk->set_first_field_offset(vk->first_field_offset_old());
6349     }
6350     ValueKlass::cast(ik)->initialize_calling_convention(CHECK);
6351   }
6352 
6353   ClassLoadingService::notify_class_loaded(ik, false /* not shared class */);
6354 
6355   if (!is_internal()) {
6356     if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, load)) {
6357       ResourceMark rm;
6358       const char* module_name = (module_entry->name() == NULL) ? UNNAMED_MODULE : module_entry->name()->as_C_string();
6359       ik->print_class_load_logging(_loader_data, module_name, _stream);
6360     }
6361 
6362     if (ik->minor_version() == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
6363         ik->major_version() == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
6364         log_is_enabled(Info, class, preview)) {
6365       ResourceMark rm;
6366       log_info(class, preview)("Loading class %s that depends on preview features (class file version %d.65535)",
6367                                ik->external_name(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
6368     }
6369 
6370     if (log_is_enabled(Debug, class, resolve))  {
6371       ResourceMark rm;
6372       // print out the superclass.
6373       const char * from = ik->external_name();
6374       if (ik->java_super() != NULL) {
6375         log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (super)",
6376                    from,
6377                    ik->java_super()->external_name());
6378       }
6379       // print out each of the interface classes referred to by this class.
6380       const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = ik->local_interfaces();
6381       if (local_interfaces != NULL) {
6382         const int length = local_interfaces->length();
6383         for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
6384           const InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
6385           const char * to = k->external_name();
6386           log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (interface)", from, to);
6387         }
6388       }
6389     }
6390   }
6391 
6392   JFR_ONLY(INIT_ID(ik);)
6393 
6394   // If we reach here, all is well.
6395   // Now remove the InstanceKlass* from the _klass_to_deallocate field
6396   // in order for it to not be destroyed in the ClassFileParser destructor.
6397   set_klass_to_deallocate(NULL);
6398 
6399   // it's official
6400   set_klass(ik);
6401 
6402   if (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6403     Universe::initialize_the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array(ik, CHECK);
6404   }
6405 
6406   debug_only(ik->verify();)
6407 }
6408 
6409 void ClassFileParser::update_class_name(Symbol* new_class_name) {
6410   // Decrement the refcount in the old name, since we're clobbering it.
6411   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6412 
6413   _class_name = new_class_name;
6414   // Increment the refcount of the new name.
6415   // Now the ClassFileParser owns this name and will decrement in
6416   // the destructor.
6417   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6418 }
6419 
6420 
6421 // For an unsafe anonymous class that is in the unnamed package, move it to its host class's
6422 // package by prepending its host class's package name to its class name and setting
6423 // its _class_name field.
6424 void ClassFileParser::prepend_host_package_name(const InstanceKlass* unsafe_anonymous_host, TRAPS) {
6425   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6426   assert(strrchr(_class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) == NULL,
6427          "Unsafe anonymous class should not be in a package");
6428   TempNewSymbol host_pkg_name =
6429     ClassLoader::package_from_class_name(unsafe_anonymous_host->name());
6430 
6431   if (host_pkg_name != NULL) {
6432     int host_pkg_len = host_pkg_name->utf8_length();
6433     int class_name_len = _class_name->utf8_length();
6434     int symbol_len = host_pkg_len + 1 + class_name_len;
6435     char* new_anon_name = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(char, symbol_len + 1);
6436     int n = os::snprintf(new_anon_name, symbol_len + 1, "%.*s/%.*s",
6437                          host_pkg_len, host_pkg_name->base(), class_name_len, _class_name->base());
6438     assert(n == symbol_len, "Unexpected number of characters in string");
6439 
6440     // Decrement old _class_name to avoid leaking.
6441     _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6442 
6443     // Create a symbol and update the anonymous class name.
6444     // The new class name is created with a refcount of one. When installed into the InstanceKlass,
6445     // it'll be two and when the ClassFileParser destructor runs, it'll go back to one and get deleted
6446     // when the class is unloaded.
6447     _class_name = SymbolTable::new_symbol(new_anon_name, symbol_len);
6448   }
6449 }
6450 
6451 // If the host class and the anonymous class are in the same package then do
6452 // nothing.  If the anonymous class is in the unnamed package then move it to its
6453 // host's package.  If the classes are in different packages then throw an IAE
6454 // exception.
6455 void ClassFileParser::fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(TRAPS) {
6456   assert(_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL, "Expected an unsafe anonymous class");
6457 
6458   const jbyte* anon_last_slash = UTF8::strrchr((const jbyte*)_class_name->base(),
6459                                                _class_name->utf8_length(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH);
6460   if (anon_last_slash == NULL) {  // Unnamed package
6461     prepend_host_package_name(_unsafe_anonymous_host, CHECK);
6462   } else {
6463     if (!_unsafe_anonymous_host->is_same_class_package(_unsafe_anonymous_host->class_loader(), _class_name)) {
6464       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6465       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalArgumentException(),
6466         err_msg("Host class %s and anonymous class %s are in different packages",
6467         _unsafe_anonymous_host->name()->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string()));
6468     }
6469   }
6470 }
6471 
6472 static bool relax_format_check_for(ClassLoaderData* loader_data) {
6473   bool trusted = (loader_data->is_the_null_class_loader_data() ||
6474                   SystemDictionary::is_platform_class_loader(loader_data->class_loader()));
6475   bool need_verify =
6476     // verifyAll
6477     (BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote) ||
6478     // verifyRemote
6479     (!BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote && !trusted);
6480   return !need_verify;
6481 }
