6483 ClassFileParser::ClassFileParser(ClassFileStream* stream,
6484                                  Symbol* name,
6485                                  ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
6486                                  Handle protection_domain,
6487                                  const InstanceKlass* unsafe_anonymous_host,
6488                                  GrowableArray<Handle>* cp_patches,
6489                                  Publicity pub_level,
6490                                  TRAPS) :
6491   _stream(stream),
6492   _requested_name(name),
6493   _class_name(NULL),
6494   _loader_data(loader_data),
6495   _unsafe_anonymous_host(unsafe_anonymous_host),
6496   _cp_patches(cp_patches),
6497   _num_patched_klasses(0),
6498   _max_num_patched_klasses(0),
6499   _orig_cp_size(0),
6500   _first_patched_klass_resolved_index(0),
6501   _super_klass(),
6502   _cp(NULL),
6503   _fields(NULL),
6504   _methods(NULL),
6505   _inner_classes(NULL),
6506   _nest_members(NULL),
6507   _nest_host(0),
6508   _record_components(NULL),
6509   _temp_local_interfaces(NULL),
6510   _local_interfaces(NULL),
6511   _transitive_interfaces(NULL),
6512   _combined_annotations(NULL),
6513   _class_annotations(NULL),
6514   _class_type_annotations(NULL),
6515   _fields_annotations(NULL),
6516   _fields_type_annotations(NULL),
6517   _klass(NULL),
6518   _klass_to_deallocate(NULL),
6519   _parsed_annotations(NULL),
6520   _fac(NULL),
6521   _field_info(NULL),
6522   _method_ordering(NULL),
6523   _all_mirandas(NULL),
6524   _vtable_size(0),
6525   _itable_size(0),
6526   _num_miranda_methods(0),
6527   _rt(REF_NONE),
6528   _protection_domain(protection_domain),
6529   _access_flags(),
6530   _pub_level(pub_level),
6531   _bad_constant_seen(0),
6532   _synthetic_flag(false),
6533   _sde_length(false),
6534   _sde_buffer(NULL),
6535   _sourcefile_index(0),
6536   _generic_signature_index(0),
6537   _major_version(0),
6538   _minor_version(0),
6539   _this_class_index(0),
6540   _super_class_index(0),
6541   _itfs_len(0),
6542   _java_fields_count(0),
6543   _need_verify(false),
6544   _relax_verify(false),
6545   _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6546   _declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6547   _has_final_method(false),
6548   _has_contended_fields(false),
6549   _has_flattenable_fields(false),
6550   _has_nonstatic_fields(false),
6551   _is_empty_inline_type(false),
6552   _is_naturally_atomic(false),
6553   _is_declared_atomic(false),
6554   _invalid_inline_super(false),
6555   _invalid_identity_super(false),
6556   _implements_identityObject(false),
6557   _has_injected_identityObject(false),
6558   _has_finalizer(false),
6559   _has_empty_finalizer(false),
6560   _has_vanilla_constructor(false),
6561   _max_bootstrap_specifier_index(-1) {
6562 
6563   _class_name = name != NULL ? name : vmSymbols::unknown_class_name();
6564   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6565 
6566   assert(THREAD->is_Java_thread(), "invariant");
6567   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
6568   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6569   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
6570   assert(_stream->buffer() == _stream->current(), "invariant");
6571   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6572   assert(0 == _access_flags.as_int(), "invariant");
6573 
6574   // Figure out whether we can skip format checking (matching classic VM behavior)
6575   if (DumpSharedSpaces) {
6576     // verify == true means it's a 'remote' class (i.e., non-boot class)
6577     // Verification decision is based on BytecodeVerificationRemote flag
6578     // for those classes.
6579     _need_verify = (stream->need_verify()) ? BytecodeVerificationRemote :
6580                                               BytecodeVerificationLocal;
6581   }
6582   else {
6583     _need_verify = Verifier::should_verify_for(_loader_data->class_loader(),
6584                                                stream->need_verify());
6585   }
6586   if (_cp_patches != NULL) {
6587     int len = _cp_patches->length();
6588     for (int i=0; i<len; i++) {
6589       if (has_cp_patch_at(i)) {
6590         Handle patch = cp_patch_at(i);
6591         if (java_lang_String::is_instance(patch()) || java_lang_Class::is_instance(patch())) {
6592           // We need to append the names of the patched classes to the end of the constant pool,
6593           // because a patched class may have a Utf8 name that's not already included in the
6594           // original constant pool. These class names are used when patch_constant_pool()
6595           // calls patch_class().
6596           //
6597           // Note that a String in cp_patch_at(i) may be used to patch a Utf8, a String, or a Class.
6598           // At this point, we don't know the tag for index i yet, because we haven't parsed the
6599           // constant pool. So we can only assume the worst -- every String is used to patch a Class.
6600           _max_num_patched_klasses++;
6601         }
6602       }
6603     }
6604   }
6605 
6606   // synch back verification state to stream
6607   stream->set_verify(_need_verify);
6608 
6609   // Check if verification needs to be relaxed for this class file
6610   // Do not restrict it to jdk1.0 or jdk1.1 to maintain backward compatibility (4982376)
6611   _relax_verify = relax_format_check_for(_loader_data);
6612 
6613   parse_stream(stream, CHECK);
6614 
6615   post_process_parsed_stream(stream, _cp, CHECK);
6616 }
6617 
6618 void ClassFileParser::clear_class_metadata() {
6619   // metadata created before the instance klass is created.  Must be
6620   // deallocated if classfile parsing returns an error.
6621   _cp = NULL;
6622   _fields = NULL;
6623   _methods = NULL;
6624   _inner_classes = NULL;
6625   _nest_members = NULL;
6626   _local_interfaces = NULL;
6627   _combined_annotations = NULL;
6628   _class_annotations = _class_type_annotations = NULL;
6629   _fields_annotations = _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
6630   _record_components = NULL;
6631 }
6632 
6633 // Destructor to clean up
6634 ClassFileParser::~ClassFileParser() {
6635   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6636 
6637   if (_cp != NULL) {
6638     MetadataFactory::free_metadata(_loader_data, _cp);
6639   }
6640   if (_fields != NULL) {
6641     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _fields);
6642   }
6643 
6644   if (_methods != NULL) {
6645     // Free methods
6646     InstanceKlass::deallocate_methods(_loader_data, _methods);
6647   }
6648 
6649   // beware of the Universe::empty_blah_array!!
6650   if (_inner_classes != NULL && _inner_classes != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6651     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _inner_classes);
6652   }
6653 
6654   if (_nest_members != NULL && _nest_members != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6655     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _nest_members);
6656   }
6657 
6658   if (_record_components != NULL) {
6659     InstanceKlass::deallocate_record_components(_loader_data, _record_components);
6660   }
6661 
6662   // Free interfaces
6663   InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(_loader_data, _super_klass,
6664                                        _local_interfaces, _transitive_interfaces);
6665 
6666   if (_combined_annotations != NULL) {
6667     // After all annotations arrays have been created, they are installed into the
6668     // Annotations object that will be assigned to the InstanceKlass being created.
6669 
6670     // Deallocate the Annotations object and the installed annotations arrays.
6671     _combined_annotations->deallocate_contents(_loader_data);
6672 
6673     // If the _combined_annotations pointer is non-NULL,
6674     // then the other annotations fields should have been cleared.
6675     assert(_class_annotations       == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6676     assert(_class_type_annotations  == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6677     assert(_fields_annotations      == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6678     assert(_fields_type_annotations == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6679   } else {
6680     // If the annotations arrays were not installed into the Annotations object,
6681     // then they have to be deallocated explicitly.
6682     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_annotations);
6683     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_type_annotations);
6684     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_annotations);
6685     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_type_annotations);
6686   }
6687 
6688   clear_class_metadata();
6689   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6690 
6691   // deallocate the klass if already created.  Don't directly deallocate, but add
6692   // to the deallocate list so that the klass is removed from the CLD::_klasses list
6693   // at a safepoint.
6694   if (_klass_to_deallocate != NULL) {
6695     _loader_data->add_to_deallocate_list(_klass_to_deallocate);
6696   }
6697 }
6698 
6699 void ClassFileParser::parse_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
6700                                    TRAPS) {
6701 
6702   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6703   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6704 
6705   // BEGIN STREAM PARSING
6706   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // magic, major, minor
6707   // Magic value
6708   const u4 magic = stream->get_u4_fast();
6709   guarantee_property(magic == JAVA_CLASSFILE_MAGIC,
6710                      "Incompatible magic value %u in class file %s",
6711                      magic, CHECK);
6712 
6713   // Version numbers
6714   _minor_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6715   _major_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6716 
6717   if (DumpSharedSpaces && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6718     ResourceMark rm;
6719     warning("Pre JDK 6 class not supported by CDS: %u.%u %s",
6720             _major_version,  _minor_version, _class_name->as_C_string());
6721     Exceptions::fthrow(
6722       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6723       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
6724       "Unsupported major.minor version for dump time %u.%u",
6725       _major_version,
6726       _minor_version);
6727   }
6728 
6729   // Check version numbers - we check this even with verifier off
6730   verify_class_version(_major_version, _minor_version, _class_name, CHECK);
6731 
6732   stream->guarantee_more(3, CHECK); // length, first cp tag
6733   u2 cp_size = stream->get_u2_fast();
6734 
6735   guarantee_property(
6736     cp_size >= 1, "Illegal constant pool size %u in class file %s",
6737     cp_size, CHECK);
6738 
6739   _orig_cp_size = cp_size;
6740   if (int(cp_size) + _max_num_patched_klasses > 0xffff) {
6741     THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_InternalError(), "not enough space for patched classes");
6742   }
6743   cp_size += _max_num_patched_klasses;
6744 
6745   _cp = ConstantPool::allocate(_loader_data,
6746                                cp_size,
6747                                CHECK);
6748 
6749   ConstantPool* const cp = _cp;
6750 
6751   parse_constant_pool(stream, cp, _orig_cp_size, CHECK);
6752 
6753   assert(cp_size == (const u2)cp->length(), "invariant");
6754 
6755   // ACCESS FLAGS
6756   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // flags, this_class, super_class, infs_len
6757 
6758   jint recognized_modifiers = JVM_RECOGNIZED_CLASS_MODIFIERS;
6759   // JVM_ACC_MODULE is defined in JDK-9 and later.
6760   if (_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION) {
6761     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_MODULE;
6762   }
6763   // JVM_ACC_VALUE is defined for class file version 55 and later
6764   if (supports_inline_types()) {
6765     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_VALUE;
6766   }
6767 
6768   // Access flags
6769   jint flags = stream->get_u2_fast() & recognized_modifiers;
6770 
6771   if ((flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE) && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6772     // Set abstract bit for old class files for backward compatibility
6773     flags |= JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT;
6774   }
6775 
6776   verify_legal_class_modifiers(flags, CHECK);
6777 
6778   short bad_constant = class_bad_constant_seen();
6779   if (bad_constant != 0) {
6780     // Do not throw CFE until after the access_flags are checked because if
6781     // ACC_MODULE is set in the access flags, then NCDFE must be thrown, not CFE.
6782     classfile_parse_error("Unknown constant tag %u in class file %s", bad_constant, CHECK);
6783   }
6784 
6785   _access_flags.set_flags(flags);
6786 
6787   // This class and superclass
6788   _this_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6789   check_property(
6790     valid_cp_range(_this_class_index, cp_size) &&
6791       cp->tag_at(_this_class_index).is_unresolved_klass(),
6792     "Invalid this class index %u in constant pool in class file %s",
6793     _this_class_index, CHECK);
6794 
6795   Symbol* const class_name_in_cp = cp->klass_name_at(_this_class_index);
6796   assert(class_name_in_cp != NULL, "class_name can't be null");
6797 
6798   // Update _class_name to reflect the name in the constant pool
6799   update_class_name(class_name_in_cp);
6800 
6801   // Don't need to check whether this class name is legal or not.
6802   // It has been checked when constant pool is parsed.
6803   // However, make sure it is not an array type.
6804   if (_need_verify) {
6805     guarantee_property(_class_name->char_at(0) != JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY,
6806                        "Bad class name in class file %s",
6807                        CHECK);
6808   }
6809 
6810   // Checks if name in class file matches requested name
6811   if (_requested_name != NULL && _requested_name != _class_name) {
6812     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6813     Exceptions::fthrow(
6814       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6815       vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
6816       "%s (wrong name: %s)",
6817       _class_name->as_C_string(),
6818       _requested_name != NULL ? _requested_name->as_C_string() : "NoName"
6819     );
6820     return;
6821   }
6822 
6823   // if this is an anonymous class fix up its name if it's in the unnamed
6824   // package.  Otherwise, throw IAE if it is in a different package than
6825   // its host class.
6826   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6827     fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(CHECK);
6828   }
6829 
6830   // Verification prevents us from creating names with dots in them, this
6831   // asserts that that's the case.
6832   assert(is_internal_format(_class_name), "external class name format used internally");
6833 
6834   if (!is_internal()) {
6835     LogTarget(Debug, class, preorder) lt;
6836     if (lt.is_enabled()){
6837       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6838       LogStream ls(lt);
6839       ls.print("%s", _class_name->as_klass_external_name());
6840       if (stream->source() != NULL) {
6841         ls.print(" source: %s", stream->source());
6842       }
6843       ls.cr();
6844     }
6845 
6846 #if INCLUDE_CDS
6847     if (DumpLoadedClassList != NULL && stream->source() != NULL && classlist_file->is_open()) {
6848       if (!ClassLoader::has_jrt_entry()) {
6849         warning("DumpLoadedClassList and CDS are not supported in exploded build");
6850         DumpLoadedClassList = NULL;
6851       } else if (SystemDictionaryShared::is_sharing_possible(_loader_data) &&
6852                  _unsafe_anonymous_host == NULL) {
6853         // Only dump the classes that can be stored into CDS archive.
6854         // Unsafe anonymous classes such as generated LambdaForm classes are also not included.
6855         oop class_loader = _loader_data->class_loader();
6856         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6857         bool skip = false;
6858         if (class_loader == NULL || SystemDictionary::is_platform_class_loader(class_loader)) {
6859           // For the boot and platform class loaders, skip classes that are not found in the
6860           // java runtime image, such as those found in the --patch-module entries.
6861           // These classes can't be loaded from the archive during runtime.
6862           if (!stream->from_boot_loader_modules_image() && strncmp(stream->source(), "jrt:", 4) != 0) {
6863             skip = true;
6864           }
6865 
6866           if (class_loader == NULL && ClassLoader::contains_append_entry(stream->source())) {
6867             // .. but don't skip the boot classes that are loaded from -Xbootclasspath/a
6868             // as they can be loaded from the archive during runtime.
6869             skip = false;
6870           }
6871         }
6872         if (skip) {
6873           tty->print_cr("skip writing class %s from source %s to classlist file",
6874             _class_name->as_C_string(), stream->source());
6875         } else {
6876           classlist_file->print_cr("%s", _class_name->as_C_string());
6877           classlist_file->flush();
6878         }
6879       }
6880     }
6881 #endif
6882   }
6883 
6884   // SUPERKLASS
6885   _super_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6886   _super_klass = parse_super_class(cp,
6887                                    _super_class_index,
6888                                    _need_verify,
6889                                    CHECK);
6890 
6891   // Interfaces
6892   _itfs_len = stream->get_u2_fast();
6893   parse_interfaces(stream,
6894                    _itfs_len,
6895                    cp,
6896                    is_inline_type(),
6897                    &_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
6898                    &_is_declared_atomic,
6899                    CHECK);
6900 
6901   assert(_temp_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
6902 
6903   // Fields (offsets are filled in later)
6904   _fac = new FieldAllocationCount();
6905   parse_fields(stream,
6906                is_interface(),
6907                is_inline_type(),
6908                _fac,
6909                cp,
6910                cp_size,
6911                &_java_fields_count,
6912                CHECK);
6913 
6914   assert(_fields != NULL, "invariant");
6915 
6916   // Methods
6917   AccessFlags promoted_flags;
6918   parse_methods(stream,
6919                 is_interface(),
6920                 is_inline_type(),
6921                 &promoted_flags,
6922                 &_has_final_method,
6923                 &_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
6924                 CHECK);
6925 
6926   assert(_methods != NULL, "invariant");
6927 
6928   // promote flags from parse_methods() to the klass' flags
6929   _access_flags.add_promoted_flags(promoted_flags.as_int());
6930 
6931   if (_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
6932     _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
6933   }
6934 
6935   // Additional attributes/annotations
6936   _parsed_annotations = new ClassAnnotationCollector();
6937   parse_classfile_attributes(stream, cp, _parsed_annotations, CHECK);
6938 
6939   assert(_inner_classes != NULL, "invariant");
6940 
6941   // Finalize the Annotations metadata object,
6942   // now that all annotation arrays have been created.
6943   create_combined_annotations(CHECK);
6944 
6945   // Make sure this is the end of class file stream
6946   guarantee_property(stream->at_eos(),
6947                      "Extra bytes at the end of class file %s",
6948                      CHECK);
6949 
6950   // all bytes in stream read and parsed
6951 }
6952 
6953 void ClassFileParser::post_process_parsed_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
6954                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
6955                                                  TRAPS) {
6956   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6957   assert(stream->at_eos(), "invariant");
6958   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
6959   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
6960 
6961   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
6962     check_property(_temp_local_interfaces->length() == 0,
6963         "java.lang.Object cannot implement an interface in class file %s",
6964         CHECK);
6965   }
6966   // We check super class after class file is parsed and format is checked
6967   if (_super_class_index > 0 && NULL ==_super_klass) {
6968     Symbol* const super_class_name = cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index);
6969     if (is_interface()) {
6970       // Before attempting to resolve the superclass, check for class format
6971       // errors not checked yet.
6972       guarantee_property(super_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object(),
6973         "Interfaces must have java.lang.Object as superclass in class file %s",
6974         CHECK);
6975     }
6976     Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
6977     _super_klass = (const InstanceKlass*)
6978                        SystemDictionary::resolve_super_or_fail(_class_name,
6979                                                                super_class_name,
6980                                                                loader,
6981                                                                _protection_domain,
6982                                                                true,
6983                                                                CHECK);
6984   }
6985 
6986   if (_super_klass != NULL) {
6987     if (_super_klass->has_nonstatic_concrete_methods()) {
6988       _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
6989     }
6990     if (_super_klass->is_declared_atomic()) {
6991       _is_declared_atomic = true;
6992     }
6993 
6994     if (_super_klass->is_interface()) {
6995       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6996       Exceptions::fthrow(
6997         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6998         vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
6999         "class %s has interface %s as super class",
7000         _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7001         _super_klass->external_name()
7002       );
7003       return;
7004     }
7005 
7006     // Make sure super class is not final
7007     if (_super_klass->is_final()) {
7008       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(), "Cannot inherit from final class");
7009     }
7010 
7011     // For an inline class, only java/lang/Object or special abstract classes
7012     // are acceptable super classes.
7013     if (is_inline_type()) {
7014       const InstanceKlass* super_ik = _super_klass;
7015       if (super_ik->invalid_inline_super()) {
7016         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7017         Exceptions::fthrow(
7018           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
7019           vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
7020           "inline class %s has an invalid super class %s",
7021           _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7022           _super_klass->external_name());
7023         return;
7024       }
7025     }
7026   }
7027 
7028   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_NonTearable() && _loader_data->class_loader() == NULL) {
7029     // This is the original source of this condition.
7030     // It propagates by inheritance, as if testing "instanceof NonTearable".
7031     _is_declared_atomic = true;
7032   } else if (*ForceNonTearable != '\0') {
7033     // Allow a command line switch to force the same atomicity property:
7034     const char* class_name_str = _class_name->as_C_string();
7035     if (StringUtils::class_list_match(ForceNonTearable, class_name_str)) {
7036       _is_declared_atomic = true;
7037     }
7038   }
7039 
7040   // Set ik->invalid_inline_super field to TRUE if already marked as invalid,
7041   // if super is marked invalid, or if is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()
7042   // returns true
7043   if (invalid_inline_super() ||
7044       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->invalid_inline_super()) ||
7045       is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()) {
7046     set_invalid_inline_super();
7047   }
7048 
7049   if (!is_inline_type() && invalid_inline_super() && (_super_klass == NULL || !_super_klass->invalid_inline_super())
7050       && !_implements_identityObject && class_name() != vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
7051     _temp_local_interfaces->append(SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass());
7052     _has_injected_identityObject = true;
7053   }
7054   int itfs_len = _temp_local_interfaces->length();
7055   if (itfs_len == 0) {
7056     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
7057   } else if (itfs_len == 1 && _temp_local_interfaces->at(0) == SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass()) {
7058     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array();
7059   } else {
7060     _local_interfaces = MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(_loader_data, itfs_len, NULL, CHECK);
7061     for (int i = 0; i < itfs_len; i++) {
7062       _local_interfaces->at_put(i, _temp_local_interfaces->at(i));
7063     }
7064   }
7065   _temp_local_interfaces = NULL;
7066   assert(_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7067 
7068   // Compute the transitive list of all unique interfaces implemented by this class
7069   _transitive_interfaces =
7070     compute_transitive_interfaces(_super_klass,
7071                                   _local_interfaces,
7072                                   _loader_data,
7073                                   CHECK);
7074 
7075   assert(_transitive_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7076 
7077   // sort methods
7078   _method_ordering = sort_methods(_methods);
7079 
7080   _all_mirandas = new GrowableArray<Method*>(20);
7081 
7082   Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
7083   klassVtable::compute_vtable_size_and_num_mirandas(&_vtable_size,
7084                                                     &_num_miranda_methods,
7085                                                     _all_mirandas,
7086                                                     _super_klass,
7087                                                     _methods,
7088                                                     _access_flags,
7089                                                     _major_version,
7090                                                     loader,
7091                                                     _class_name,
7092                                                     _local_interfaces,
7093                                                     CHECK);
7094 
7095   // Size of Java itable (in words)
7096   _itable_size = is_interface() ? 0 :
7097     klassItable::compute_itable_size(_transitive_interfaces);
7098 
7099   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
7100   assert(_parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
7101 
7102 
7103   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
7104     if (fs.is_flattenable() && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
7105       // Pre-load value class
7106       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::resolve_flattenable_field_or_fail(&fs,
7107           Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
7108           _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
7109       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
7110       assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(), "Inline type expected");
7111       _has_flattenable_fields = true;
7112     }
7113   }
7114 
7115   _field_info = new FieldLayoutInfo();
7116   if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
7117     FieldLayoutBuilder lb(class_name(), super_klass(), _cp, _fields,
7118         _parsed_annotations->is_contended(), is_inline_type(),
7119         loader_data(), _protection_domain, _field_info);
7120     lb.build_layout(CHECK);
7121     if (is_inline_type()) {
7122       _alignment = lb.get_alignment();
7123       _first_field_offset = lb.get_first_field_offset();
7124       _exact_size_in_bytes = lb.get_exact_size_in_byte();
7125     }
7126   } else {
7127     layout_fields(cp, _fac, _parsed_annotations, _field_info, CHECK);
7128   }
7129 
7130   // Compute reference type
7131   _rt = (NULL ==_super_klass) ? REF_NONE : _super_klass->reference_type();
7132 }
7133 
7134 void ClassFileParser::set_klass(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7135 
7136 #ifdef ASSERT
7137   if (klass != NULL) {
7138     assert(NULL == _klass, "leaking?");
7139   }
7140 #endif
7141 
7142   _klass = klass;
7143 }
7144 
7145 void ClassFileParser::set_klass_to_deallocate(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7146 
7147 #ifdef ASSERT
7148   if (klass != NULL) {
7149     assert(NULL == _klass_to_deallocate, "leaking?");
7150   }
7151 #endif
7152 
7153   _klass_to_deallocate = klass;
7154 }
7155 
7156 // Caller responsible for ResourceMark
7157 // clone stream with rewound position
7158 const ClassFileStream* ClassFileParser::clone_stream() const {
7159   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
7160 
7161   return _stream->clone();
7162 }
7163 
7164 // ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
7165 // debugging
7166 
7167 #ifdef ASSERT
7168 
7169 // return true if class_name contains no '.' (internal format is '/')
7170 bool ClassFileParser::is_internal_format(Symbol* class_name) {
7171   if (class_name != NULL) {
7172     ResourceMark rm;
7173     char* name = class_name->as_C_string();
7174     return strchr(name, JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT) == NULL;
7175   } else {
7176     return true;
7177   }
7178 }
7179 
7180 #endif
